```markdown
# Full Stack Software Engineer - ML Cloud Applications
# üéØ HR SCREEN HIGHLIGHTS

---

## Company Overview

### Electronic Arts
Electronic Arts creates next-level entertainment experiences that inspire players and fans around the world. Here, everyone is part of the story. Part of a community that connects across the globe. A place where creativity thrives, new perspectives are invited, and ideas matter. A team where everyone makes play happen.

### EA Experiences
Our EA Experiences group is dedicated to ensuring great experiences for our growing communities centered around our world-renowned brands, including fan-favorites like **Apex, Battlefield, EA SPORTS FC, Madden NFL and The Sims**, just to name a few. We're a multi-functional group, with world-class expertise building fandoms, driving interactive storytelling, and positioning our franchises at the center of the broader entertainment ecosystem. We inspire, connect, and engage fans through culturally relevant content, intentionally architected journeys across channels, and meaningful fan care. Our goal is to provide valuable, easy experiences that fans love ‚Äì in our games, around our games, and through innovative adjacent experiences to grow and enrich how fans experience EA as we shape the future of entertainment.

### Fan Growth
EA's Fan Growth organization is responsible for **elevating the experiences customers get from our entertainment and maximizing their fun**. We're obsessed with the experiences our fans have with EA. We value people who bring new ideas and perspectives to make Fan Growth a great place to be and be from. **We celebrate inclusion**. It's just as important for us to create great experiences for our people as for our players. We're looking for people who will **show up excited to work and ready for fun**.

---

## Position Summary
‚≠ê **KEY ROLE**: The Full Stack Software Engineer - ML Cloud Applications designs, develops, and maintains **fast, scalable, cloud-based applications** that take full advantage of existing **ML/Generative AI technologies**. This includes building **full-stack AI-driven solutions and automation pipelines** that accelerate product development cycles and enable rapid experimentation. This position **collaborates closely** with many cross-functional partners such as **tech artists, content creators, data scientists, writers, and game engine programmers** to streamline model deployment, optimize infrastructure, and deliver reliable, high-performance applications powered by modern cloud and AI technologies.

---

## Work Arrangement & Benefits
- **Location**: üè¢ **On-site or hybrid role with 3 days a week in office**
- **Reporting**: Sr. Technology Lead in the **Marketing Content Production Craft team**
- **Benefits**: Health coverage with health care spending, retirement savings plan, gym access, **free games**, and plenty of additional perks!

---

## üéØ Responsibilities (FOCUS AREAS)
- ‚úÖ Analyzing user requirements and technical constraints to design and implement efficient **machine learning application solutions on the cloud**
- ‚úÖ **Leveraging and integrating AWS services** (e.g., **Lambda, Cognito, SAM, SSM, SageMaker, API Gateway, DynamoDB, CloudWatch**, etc.) and **AI/ML tools** to enable fast development and deployment of intelligent applications
- ‚úÖ Delivering **robust, scalable, and maintainable cloud-native applications** using modern development frameworks, tools, and best practices
- ‚úÖ **Autonomously architecting and building end-to-end pipelines** that handle **data ingestion, model inference, and real-time API services**
- ‚úÖ Generating **technical documentation**
- ‚úÖ **Collaborating with partner teams** in developing shared solutions across different EA domains

---

## üö® Required Qualifications (MUST MENTION)
- ‚úÖ **Experience**: **4+ years** of professional software development experience building **cloud-native applications** (web, API services, ML pipelines)
- ‚úÖ **Programming**: **Strong proficiency in Python**, with experience using **ML libraries and frameworks**
- ‚úÖ **Version Control**: Expertise with source control software like Perforce or **Git**
- ‚úÖ **Cloud Platform**: Experience developing on **AWS** using services such as **Lambda, SAM, SSM, SageMaker, API Gateway, DynamoDB**, etc.
- ‚úÖ **AI Tools**: Experience with **AI tools for fast application development** (coding agents, AWS, **MCP**, **n8n**‚Ä¶)
- ‚úÖ **Development Stack**: Experience with **full-stack or backend development** including **RESTful APIs** and **infrastructure-as-code tools (CloudFormation)**

---

## üéØ YOUR STRENGTHS TO HIGHLIGHT
1. **5+ years at Amazon** building cloud-native applications
2. **AWS expertise**: Lambda, SageMaker, DynamoDB, API Gateway, CloudWatch, Step Functions, AWS CDK/CloudFormation
3. **Python + ML**: Built AI agents, RAG systems, NLP solutions
4. **Full-stack**: React, TypeScript, FastAPI, Flask
5. **AI tools**: Extensive experience with coding agents (Cursor, Windsurf), MCP, n8n
6. **Documentation**: Led org-wide documentation initiatives
7. **Cross-functional collaboration**: Led teams of 8+ engineers, designers, data scientists
```

```markdown
# HR Screen Prep Guide - Electronic Arts
## Full Stack Software Engineer - ML Cloud Applications

**Interviewer**: Tyler (HR Recruiter)  
**Company**: Electronic Arts  
**Role**: Full Stack Software Engineer - ML Cloud Applications  
**Team**: Marketing Content Production Craft Team (Fan Growth Organization)

---

## üéØ Quick Reference - Key Match Points

| **Requirement** | **Your Experience** |
|-----------------|---------------------|
| 4+ years cloud development | ‚úÖ 5+ years at Amazon building AWS cloud-native apps |
| Python + ML proficiency | ‚úÖ Built AI agents, RAG systems, NLP chatbots, ML pipelines |
| AWS services (Lambda, SageMaker, DynamoDB, API Gateway) | ‚úÖ Extensive: Led teams using Lambda, SageMaker, DynamoDB, API Gateway, Step Functions, CDK, CloudWatch |
| AI tools (coding agents, MCP, n8n) | ‚úÖ Heavy user of Cursor, Windsurf, MCP, n8n |
| Full-stack development | ‚úÖ React, TypeScript, Flask, FastAPI, Node.js |
| IaC (CloudFormation) | ‚úÖ AWS CDK & CloudFormation expert, built 4-stage CI/CD pipelines |
| Technical documentation | ‚úÖ Led org-wide documentation workshop at Amazon |
| Cross-functional collaboration | ‚úÖ Led teams of 8 engineers, designers, data scientists |

---

## üìã Common HR Screen Questions & Answers

### 1. "Tell me about yourself"
**Answer (60-90 seconds)**:
"I'm a software engineer with 5+ years of experience at Amazon building cloud-native ML applications. I specialize in full-stack AI-driven solutions using AWS services like Lambda, SageMaker, DynamoDB, and API Gateway. 

At Amazon, I led a team of 8 engineers building serverless data pipelines processing 40TB/day, serving 40M+ monthly customers. I also built internal-documentation-powered AI agents that improved resolution time by 82% and saved 240+ dev-hours per month.

Outside Amazon, I've been deeply focused on AI development‚Äîbuilding voice assistants, real-time transcription tools, health misinformation prevention systems, and full-stack AI applications. I'm excited about EA's role because it combines my passion for AI/ML, cloud architecture, and creating engaging experiences that millions of people use."

### 2. "Why are you interested in Electronic Arts?"
**Answer**:
"Three main reasons:
1. **Impact at scale**: EA's games reach hundreds of millions of fans globally. Building ML-powered cloud applications that enhance these experiences is incredibly exciting.
2. **Technical alignment**: The role perfectly matches my expertise‚ÄîPython, AWS (Lambda, SageMaker, DynamoDB), AI tools, full-stack development, and IaC with CloudFormation. I've built exactly these types of systems at Amazon.
3. **Innovation & collaboration**: Working with tech artists, data scientists, content creators, and game developers to deploy ML models and build automation pipelines aligns with my experience leading cross-functional teams and my passion for AI-driven solutions."

### 3. "Why are you leaving Amazon?"
**Answer**:
"I left Amazon in March 2025 after 5+ years to focus on specialized AI development work. Amazon gave me incredible experience building cloud-native applications at massive scale, but I'm now looking for opportunities to dive deeper into ML/AI-driven applications‚Äîwhich is exactly what this EA role offers. I want to work on innovative AI solutions that directly enhance user experiences, and EA's Fan Growth organization is doing exactly that."

### 4. "What's your biggest accomplishment?"
**Answer**:
"At Amazon, I built AI agents powered by internal documentation that answered CI/CD admin questions instantly. This improved resolution time by 82% and projected savings of 240+ dev-hours per month. What made it special was the end-to-end ownership‚ÄîI identified the problem, architected the solution using AWS Lambda and SageMaker, built the RAG pipeline, and drove adoption across the org. It demonstrated my ability to combine ML/AI with cloud infrastructure to solve real business problems‚Äîexactly what this EA role requires."

### 5. "What's your experience with AWS services mentioned in the JD?"
**Answer**:
"Extensive hands-on experience:
- **Lambda & API Gateway**: Built serverless APIs and data pipelines
- **SageMaker**: Deployed ML models (Endpoints, Batch Transform)
- **DynamoDB**: Session persistence, high-throughput data storage
- **CloudWatch & X-Ray**: Built 4-stage CI/CD pipelines with granular monitoring
- **AWS CDK/CloudFormation**: Infrastructure-as-code expert, architected entire deployment pipelines
- **Cognito**: Integrated authentication systems
- **SAM & SSM**: Used for serverless app deployment and parameter management
- **Step Functions**: Orchestrated complex workflows for 40TB/day data processing"

### 6. "What's your experience with AI tools like MCP, n8n, coding agents?"
**Answer**:
"I'm a power user of modern AI development tools:
- **Coding agents**: Daily user of Cursor and Windsurf for AI-assisted development
- **MCP (Model Context Protocol)**: Familiar with the architecture and use cases
- **n8n**: Experience with workflow automation
- **Generative AI platforms**: OpenAI, Anthropic, Gemini, Ollama
- **Real-world application**: Built 'Bob', my personal AI voice assistant with 8 operational modes, reducing platform costs by 40x through prompt engineering

These tools are central to my workflow and I'm excited to leverage them to accelerate EA's product development cycles."

### 7. "How do you handle working with cross-functional teams?"
**Answer**:
"At Amazon, I led teams of 8 engineers, designers, and data scientists. Key practices:
1. **Clear communication**: Led org-wide documentation workshops, ensuring everyone had access to technical reference materials
2. **Stakeholder management**: Collaborated with product managers, data scientists, and external teams
3. **Empowerment**: Enabled team autonomy while maintaining alignment on goals
4. **Documentation**: Created comprehensive technical documentation for every project

This aligns perfectly with the EA role's need to work with tech artists, content creators, data scientists, and game engine programmers."

### 8. "What are your salary expectations?"
**Answer**:
"I'm looking for a competitive package that reflects my 5+ years of experience building cloud-native ML applications at Amazon. I'm open to discussing the full compensation package including base, equity, and benefits. What range does EA typically offer for this role?"

### 9. "What's your availability?"
**Answer**:
"I'm available immediately and flexible with the hybrid arrangement (3 days/week in office). I'm based in Vancouver, BC."

### 10. "Do you have any questions for me?"
**See Questions to Ask section below**

---

## üí° Key Talking Points - Memorize These

### Your AWS Expertise (Match to JD)
- **Lambda**: Serverless API development, event-driven architectures
- **SageMaker**: Model deployment (Endpoints, Batch Transform)
- **DynamoDB**: High-throughput NoSQL database for session persistence
- **API Gateway**: RESTful API development and management
- **CloudWatch & X-Ray**: Monitoring, logging, distributed tracing
- **AWS CDK/CloudFormation**: Infrastructure-as-code, CI/CD pipelines
- **Cognito**: Authentication and authorization
- **SAM & SSM**: Serverless Application Model, Systems Manager
- **Step Functions**: Workflow orchestration

### Your AI/ML Experience (Match to JD)
- Built AI agents for documentation Q&A (RAG pipeline)
- Deployed NLP chatbots with full CI/CD
- Integrated OpenAI Whisper for local ML-based speech recognition
- Health misinformation prevention system with multi-agent simulation
- Experience with OpenAI, Anthropic, Gemini, Ollama
- Vector databases, RAG, LLMs, model deployment

### Your Full-Stack Expertise (Match to JD)
- **Frontend**: React 19, TypeScript
- **Backend**: Python (Flask, FastAPI), Node.js
- **Databases**: DynamoDB, PostgreSQL, SQLite
- **APIs**: RESTful API design and implementation
- **CI/CD**: GitHub Actions, AWS CDK pipelines
- **IaC**: AWS CDK, CloudFormation

### Your Documentation & Collaboration (Match to JD)
- Led org-wide documentation workshop at Amazon
- "Robust documentation & operational readiness" recognition
- Led teams of 8 engineers, designers, data scientists
- Cross-functional collaboration with multiple teams

### Your AI Development Tools (Match to JD)
- **Coding agents**: Cursor, Windsurf (daily use)
- **MCP**: Model Context Protocol familiarity
- **n8n**: Workflow automation
- **OpenAI, Anthropic, Gemini**: API integration experience

## üö® Red Flags to Avoid

‚ùå **Don't say**:
- Negative things about Amazon or previous employers
- "I don't have experience with X" (reframe as "I haven't used X specifically, but I've used similar tools like Y")
- Appear desperate or over-eager
- Discuss compensation too early (let them bring it up)

‚úÖ **Do say**:
- Specific examples with metrics (82% improvement, 240 dev-hours saved, 40TB/day)
- "That's a great question" (buy yourself thinking time)
- Ask clarifying questions if needed
- Express genuine excitement about EA's mission
```

```markdown
# HR Screen Prep Guide - Electronic Arts
## Full Stack Software Engineer - ML Cloud Applications

**Interviewer**: Tyler Poe (HR Recruiter)  
**Company**: Electronic Arts  
**Role**: Full Stack Software Engineer - ML Cloud Applications  
**Team**: Marketing Content Production Craft Team (Fan Growth Organization)

---

## üéØ Quick Reference - Key Match Points

| **Requirement** | **Your Experience** |
|-----------------|---------------------|
| 4+ years cloud development | ‚úÖ 5+ years at Amazon building AWS cloud-native apps |
| Python + ML proficiency | ‚úÖ Built AI agents, RAG systems, NLP chatbots, ML pipelines |
| AWS services (Lambda, SageMaker, DynamoDB, API Gateway) | ‚úÖ Extensive: Led teams using Lambda, SageMaker, DynamoDB, API Gateway, Step Functions, CDK, CloudWatch |
| AI tools (coding agents, MCP, n8n) | ‚úÖ Heavy user of Cursor, Windsurf, MCP, n8n |
| Full-stack development | ‚úÖ React, TypeScript, Flask, FastAPI, Node.js |
| IaC (CloudFormation) | ‚úÖ AWS CDK & CloudFormation expert, built 4-stage CI/CD pipelines |
| Technical documentation | ‚úÖ Led org-wide documentation workshop at Amazon |
| Cross-functional collaboration | ‚úÖ Led teams of 8 engineers, designers, data scientists |

---

## üìã Common HR Screen Questions & Answers

### 1. "Tell me about yourself"
**Answer (60-90 seconds)**:
"I'm a software engineer with 5+ years of experience at Amazon building cloud-native ML applications. I specialize in full-stack AI-driven solutions using AWS services like Lambda, SageMaker, DynamoDB, and API Gateway. 

At Amazon, I led a team of 8 engineers building serverless data pipelines processing 40TB/day, serving 40M+ monthly customers. I also built internal-documentation-powered AI agents that improved resolution time by 82% and saved 240+ dev-hours per month.

Outside Amazon, I've been deeply focused on AI development‚Äîbuilding voice assistants, real-time transcription tools, health misinformation prevention systems, and full-stack AI applications. I'm excited about EA's role because it combines my passion for AI/ML, cloud architecture, and creating engaging experiences that millions of people use."

### 2. "Why are you interested in Electronic Arts?"
**Answer**:
"Three main reasons:
1. **Impact at scale**: EA's games reach hundreds of millions of fans globally. Building ML-powered cloud applications that enhance these experiences is incredibly exciting.
2. **Technical alignment**: The role perfectly matches my expertise‚ÄîPython, AWS (Lambda, SageMaker, DynamoDB), AI tools, full-stack development, and IaC with CloudFormation. I've built exactly these types of systems at Amazon.
3. **Innovation & collaboration**: Working with tech artists, data scientists, content creators, and game developers to deploy ML models and build automation pipelines aligns with my experience leading cross-functional teams and my passion for AI-driven solutions."

### 3. "Why are you leaving Amazon?" / "What have you been doing since March?"
**Answer**:
"My team and I were laid off in March 2025 as part of organizational restructuring. After 5+ years at Amazon, I took that as an opportunity to take a step back and spend quality time with family‚Äîsomething I hadn't prioritized during my intense years at Amazon. For example, I was able to be present for important family milestones and reconnect with loved ones.

I also used that time productively to deepen my ML/AI expertise. I enrolled in a comprehensive Machine Learning program covering EDA & Feature Engineering, Model Evaluation, Neural Networks, NLP, and Agentic Frameworks. I built several full-stack AI applications including voice assistants, real-time transcription tools, and health misinformation prevention systems‚Äîall leveraging AWS, Python, and modern AI tools.

Now I'm energized and ready to bring that expanded skillset to a role like this at EA, where I can build ML-powered cloud applications that enhance experiences for millions of fans."

### 4. "What's your biggest accomplishment?"
**Answer**:
"At Amazon, I built AI agents powered by internal documentation that answered CI/CD admin questions instantly. This improved resolution time by 82% and projected savings of 240+ dev-hours per month. What made it special was the end-to-end ownership‚ÄîI identified the problem, architected the solution using AWS Lambda and SageMaker, built the RAG pipeline, and drove adoption across the org. It demonstrated my ability to combine ML/AI with cloud infrastructure to solve real business problems‚Äîexactly what this EA role requires."

### 5. "What's your experience with AWS services mentioned in the JD?"
**Answer**:
"Extensive hands-on experience:
- **Lambda & API Gateway**: Built serverless APIs and data pipelines
- **SageMaker**: Deployed ML models (Endpoints, Batch Transform)
- **DynamoDB**: Session persistence, high-throughput data storage
- **CloudWatch & X-Ray**: Built 4-stage CI/CD pipelines with granular monitoring
- **AWS CDK/CloudFormation**: Infrastructure-as-code expert, architected entire deployment pipelines
- **Cognito**: Integrated authentication systems
- **SAM & SSM**: Used for serverless app deployment and parameter management
- **Step Functions**: Orchestrated complex workflows for 40TB/day data processing"

### 6. "What's your experience with AI tools like MCP, n8n, coding agents?"
**Answer**:
"I'm a power user of modern AI development tools:
- **Coding agents**: Daily user of Cursor and Windsurf for AI-assisted development
- **MCP (Model Context Protocol)**: Familiar with the architecture and use cases
- **n8n**: Experience with workflow automation
- **Generative AI platforms**: OpenAI, Anthropic, Gemini, Ollama
- **Real-world application**: Built 'Bob', my personal AI voice assistant with 8 operational modes, reducing platform costs by 40x through prompt engineering

These tools are central to my workflow and I'm excited to leverage them to accelerate EA's product development cycles."

### 7. "How do you handle working with cross-functional teams?"
**Answer**:
"At Amazon, I led teams of 8 engineers, designers, and data scientists. Key practices:
1. **Clear communication**: Led org-wide documentation workshops, ensuring everyone had access to technical reference materials
2. **Stakeholder management**: Collaborated with product managers, data scientists, and external teams
3. **Empowerment**: Enabled team autonomy while maintaining alignment on goals
4. **Documentation**: Created comprehensive technical documentation for every project

This aligns perfectly with the EA role's need to work with tech artists, content creators, data scientists, and game engine programmers."

### 8. "What are your salary expectations?"
**Answer**:
"I'm looking for a competitive package that reflects my 5+ years of experience building cloud-native ML applications at Amazon. I'm open to discussing the full compensation package including base, equity, and benefits. What range does EA typically offer for this role?"

### 9. "What's your availability?"
**Answer**:
"I'm available immediately and flexible with the hybrid arrangement (3 days/week in office). I'm based in Vancouver, BC."

### 10. "Do you have any questions for me?"
**See Questions to Ask section below**

---

## üí° Key Talking Points - Memorize These

### Your AWS Expertise (Match to JD)
- **Lambda**: Serverless API development, event-driven architectures
- **SageMaker**: Model deployment (Endpoints, Batch Transform)
- **DynamoDB**: High-throughput NoSQL database for session persistence
- **API Gateway**: RESTful API development and management
- **CloudWatch & X-Ray**: Monitoring, logging, distributed tracing
- **AWS CDK/CloudFormation**: Infrastructure-as-code, CI/CD pipelines
- **Cognito**: Authentication and authorization
- **SAM & SSM**: Serverless Application Model, Systems Manager
- **Step Functions**: Workflow orchestration

### Your AI/ML Experience (Match to JD)
- Built AI agents for documentation Q&A (RAG pipeline)
- Deployed NLP chatbots with full CI/CD
- Integrated OpenAI Whisper for local ML-based speech recognition
- Health misinformation prevention system with multi-agent simulation
- Experience with OpenAI, Anthropic, Gemini, Ollama
- Vector databases, RAG, LLMs, model deployment

### Your Full-Stack Expertise (Match to JD)
- **Frontend**: React 19, TypeScript
- **Backend**: Python (Flask, FastAPI), Node.js
- **Databases**: DynamoDB, PostgreSQL, SQLite
- **APIs**: RESTful API design and implementation
- **CI/CD**: GitHub Actions, AWS CDK pipelines
- **IaC**: AWS CDK, CloudFormation

### Your Documentation & Collaboration (Match to JD)
- Led org-wide documentation workshop at Amazon
- "Robust documentation & operational readiness" recognition
- Led teams of 8 engineers, designers, data scientists
- Cross-functional collaboration with multiple teams

### Your AI Development Tools (Match to JD)
- **Coding agents**: Cursor, Windsurf (daily use)
- **MCP**: Model Context Protocol familiarity
- **n8n**: Workflow automation
- **OpenAI, Anthropic, Gemini**: API integration experience

---

## ‚ùì Questions to Ask Tyler (HR Recruiter)

### About the Role
1. "What does a typical day look like for this position?"
2. "Who would I be collaborating with most closely? (tech artists, data scientists, game developers?)"
3. "What ML/AI projects is the team currently working on or planning?"
4. "What AWS services does the team use most heavily?"

### About the Team
5. "Can you tell me more about the Marketing Content Production Craft team?"
6. "How large is the Fan Growth organization?"
7. "What's the team culture like?"

### About Next Steps
8. "What does the interview process look like after this screen?"
9. "When are you looking to have someone start?"
10. "What's the timeline for next steps?"

### About EA
11. "What makes EA's Fan Growth organization unique compared to other parts of EA?"
12. "How does EA support professional development and learning?"

---

## üö® Red Flags to Avoid

‚ùå **Don't say**:
- Negative things about Amazon or previous employers
- "I don't have experience with X" (reframe as "I haven't used X specifically, but I've used similar tools like Y")
- Appear desperate or over-eager
- Discuss compensation too early (let them bring it up)

‚úÖ **Do say**:
- Specific examples with metrics (82% improvement, 240 dev-hours saved, 40TB/day)
- "That's a great question" (buy yourself thinking time)
- Ask clarifying questions if needed
- Express genuine excitement about EA's mission

---

## üìû Call Logistics Prep

- **Test your setup**: Camera, microphone, internet connection
- **Quiet environment**: No interruptions
- **Have ready**: Resume, JD, this prep guide, notepad
- **Professional background**: Clean, well-lit space
- **Dress code**: Business casual (collared shirt minimum)
- **Join 2-3 minutes early**: Never be late

---

## üéØ Closing Statement

"Thank you for taking the time to speak with me today, Tyler. I'm really excited about this opportunity. The role aligns perfectly with my experience building cloud-native ML applications at Amazon, and I'm particularly drawn to EA's mission of creating engaging experiences for millions of fans. I'm confident I can hit the ground running with AWS, Python, and AI tools to help accelerate the Fan Growth team's product development cycles. I look forward to the next steps!"

You are an **excellent match** for this role:
- ‚úÖ 5+ years experience (exceeds 4+ requirement)

- ‚úÖ IaC (AWS CDK/CloudFormation)

- ‚úÖ Cross-functional team leadership
- ‚úÖ Hybrid work arrangement compatible
```

```markdown
- **Step Functions**: Orchestrated complex workflows for 40TB/day data processing"

### 6. "What's your experience with AI tools like MCP, n8n, coding agents?"
**Answer**:
"I'm a power user of modern AI development tools:
- **Coding agents**: Daily user of Cursor and Windsurf for AI-assisted development
- **MCP (Model Context Protocol)**: Familiar with the architecture and use cases
- **n8n**: Experience with workflow automation
- **Generative AI platforms**: OpenAI, Anthropic, Gemini, Ollama
- **Real-world application**: Built 'Bob', my personal AI voice assistant with 8 operational modes, reducing platform costs by 40x through prompt engineering

These tools are central to my workflow and I'm excited to leverage them to accelerate EA's product development cycles."

### 7. "How do you handle working with cross-functional teams?"
**Answer**:
"At Amazon, I led teams of 8 engineers, designers, and data scientists. Key practices:
1. **Clear communication**: Led org-wide documentation workshops, ensuring everyone had access to technical reference materials
2. **Stakeholder management**: Collaborated with product managers, data scientists, and external teams
3. **Empowerment**: Enabled team autonomy while maintaining alignment on goals
4. **Documentation**: Created comprehensive technical documentation for every project

This aligns perfectly with the EA role's need to work with tech artists, content creators, data scientists, and game engine programmers."

### 8. "What are your salary expectations?"
**Answer**:
"I'm looking for a competitive package that reflects my 5+ years of experience building cloud-native ML applications at Amazon. I'm open to discussing the full compensation package including base, equity, and benefits. What range does EA typically offer for this role?"

### 9. "What's your availability?"
**Answer**:
"I'm available immediately and flexible with the hybrid arrangement (3 days/week in office). I'm based in Vancouver, BC."

### 10. "Do you have any questions for me?"
**See Questions to Ask section below**
```

```markdown
# HR Screen Prep Guide - Electronic Arts
## Full Stack Software Engineer - ML Cloud Applications

**Interviewer**: Tyler Poe (HR Recruiter)  
**Company**: Electronic Arts  
**Role**: Full Stack Software Engineer - ML Cloud Applications  
**Team**: Marketing Content Production Craft Team (Fan Growth Organization)

---

## üí° Employment Gap Strategy

**Approach**: Be transparent and authentic
- ‚úÖ **Mention layoff**: "My team and I were laid off in March 2025" (ownership, not personal failure)
- ‚úÖ **Family time**: Spent quality time with family, present for important milestones
- ‚úÖ **Productive learning**: Enrolled in ML program, built full-stack AI applications
- ‚úÖ **Ready & energized**: Expanded skillset, ready to contribute

**Key message**: Turned a challenging situation into an opportunity for growth and family

---

## üéØ Quick Reference - Key Match Points

| **Requirement** | **Your Experience** |
|-----------------|---------------------|
| 4+ years cloud development | ‚úÖ 5+ years at Amazon building AWS cloud-native apps |
| Python + ML proficiency | ‚úÖ Built AI agents, RAG systems, NLP chatbots, ML pipelines |
| AWS services (Lambda, SageMaker, DynamoDB, API Gateway) | ‚úÖ Extensive: Led teams using Lambda, SageMaker, DynamoDB, API Gateway, Step Functions, CDK, CloudWatch |
| AI tools (coding agents, MCP, n8n) | ‚úÖ Heavy user of Cursor, Windsurf, MCP, n8n |
| Full-stack development | ‚úÖ React, TypeScript, Flask, FastAPI, Node.js |

## üìã Common HR Screen Questions & Answers

### 1. "Tell me about yourself"
**Answer (60-90 seconds)**:
"I'm a software engineer with 5+ years of experience at Amazon building cloud-native ML applications. I specialize in full-stack AI-driven solutions using AWS services like Lambda, SageMaker, DynamoDB, and API Gateway. 

At Amazon, I led a team of 8 engineers building serverless data pipelines processing 40TB/day, serving 40M+ monthly customers. I also built internal-documentation-powered AI agents that improved resolution time by 82% and saved 240+ dev-hours per month.

Outside Amazon, I've been deeply focused on AI development‚Äîbuilding voice assistants, real-time transcription tools, health misinformation prevention systems, and full-stack AI applications. I'm excited about EA's role because it combines my passion for AI/ML, cloud architecture, and creating engaging experiences that millions of people use."

### 2. "Why are you interested in Electronic Arts?"
**Answer**:
"Three main reasons:
1. **Impact at scale**: EA's games reach hundreds of millions of fans globally. Building ML-powered cloud applications that enhance these experiences is incredibly exciting.
2. **Technical alignment**: The role perfectly matches my expertise‚ÄîPython, AWS (Lambda, SageMaker, DynamoDB), AI tools, full-stack development, and IaC with CloudFormation. I've built exactly these types of systems at Amazon.
3. **Innovation & collaboration**: Working with tech artists, data scientists, content creators, and game developers to deploy ML models and build automation pipelines aligns with my experience leading cross-functional teams and my passion for AI-driven solutions."

### 3. "Why are you leaving Amazon?" / "What have you been doing since March?"
**Answer**:
```
```markdown
"My **team** and I were **laid off** in **March 2025** as part of **organizational restructuring**. My manager, manager's manager‚Äîwe were all laid off together. Our **Beauty Tech team** was being **merged** into a different team.

After **5+ years** at Amazon, I took that as an opportunity to **take a step back**. I used that time to **work on myself** and spend quality time with **family**. It was a good break.

I also used that time **productively** to deepen my **ML/AI expertise**. I enrolled in a comprehensive **Machine Learning program** covering **EDA**, **Feature Engineering**, **Neural Networks**, **NLP**, and **Agentic Frameworks**.

I built several **full-stack AI applications**‚Äî**voice assistants**, **real-time transcription tools**, and **health misinformation prevention systems**. All leveraging **AWS**, **Python**, and modern **AI tools**.

Now I'm **energized** and ready to bring that expanded skillset to a role like this at EA. I want to build **ML-powered cloud applications** that enhance experiences for **millions of fans**."

### 4. "What's your biggest accomplishment?"
**Answer**:
"At Amazon, I built AI agents powered by internal documentation that answered CI/CD admin questions instantly. This improved resolution time by 82% and projected savings of 240+ dev-hours per month. What made it special was the end-to-end ownership‚ÄîI identified the problem, architected the solution using AWS Lambda and SageMaker, built the RAG pipeline, and drove adoption across the org. It demonstrated my ability to combine ML/AI with cloud infrastructure to solve real business problems‚Äîexactly what this EA role requires."

### 5. "What's your experience with AWS services mentioned in the JD?"
**Answer**:
"Extensive hands-on experience:
- **Lambda & API Gateway**: Built serverless APIs and data pipelines
- **SageMaker**: Deployed ML models (Endpoints, Batch Transform)
- **DynamoDB**: Session persistence, high-throughput data storage
- **CloudWatch & X-Ray**: Built 4-stage CI/CD pipelines with granular monitoring
- **AWS CDK/CloudFormation**: Infrastructure-as-code expert, architected entire deployment pipelines
- **Cognito**: Integrated authentication systems
- **SAM & SSM**: Used for serverless app deployment and parameter management
- **Step Functions**: Orchestrated complex workflows for 40TB/day data processing"

### 6. "What's your experience with AI tools like MCP, n8n, coding agents?"
**Answer**:
"I'm a power user of modern AI development tools:
- **Coding agents**: Daily user of Cursor and Windsurf for AI-assisted development
- **MCP (Model Context Protocol)**: Familiar with the architecture and use cases
- **n8n**: Experience with workflow automation
- **Generative AI platforms**: OpenAI, Anthropic, Gemini, Ollama
- **Real-world application**: Built 'Bob', my personal AI voice assistant with 8 operational modes, reducing platform costs by 40x through prompt engineering

These tools are central to my workflow and I'm excited to leverage them to accelerate EA's product development cycles."

### 7. "How do you handle working with cross-functional teams?"
**Answer**:
"At Amazon, I led teams of 8 engineers, designers, and data scientists. Key practices:
1. **Clear communication**: Led org-wide documentation workshops, ensuring everyone had access to technical reference materials
2. **Stakeholder management**: Collaborated with product managers, data scientists, and external teams
3. **Empowerment**: Enabled team autonomy while maintaining alignment on goals
4. **Documentation**: Created comprehensive technical documentation for every project

This aligns perfectly with the EA role's need to work with tech artists, content creators, data scientists, and game engine programmers."

### 8. "What are your salary expectations?"
**Answer**:
"I'm looking for a competitive package that reflects my 5+ years of experience building cloud-native ML applications at Amazon. I'm open to discussing the full compensation package including base, equity, and benefits. What range does EA typically offer for this role?"

### 9. "What's your availability?"
**Answer**:
"I'm available immediately and flexible with the hybrid arrangement (3 days/week in office). I'm based in Vancouver, BC."

**See Questions to Ask section below**

- **Backend**: Python (Flask, FastAPI), Node.js
- **Databases**: DynamoDB, PostgreSQL, SQLite
- **APIs**: RESTful API design and implementation
- **CI/CD**: GitHub Actions, AWS CDK pipelines
- **IaC**: AWS CDK, CloudFormation

### Your Documentation & Collaboration (Match to JD)
- Led org-wide documentation workshop at Amazon
- "Robust documentation & operational readiness" recognition
- Led teams of 8 engineers, designers, data scientists
- Cross-functional collaboration with multiple teams

### Your AI Development Tools (Match to JD)
- **Coding agents**: Cursor, Windsurf (daily use)
- **MCP**: Model Context Protocol familiarity
- **n8n**: Workflow automation
- **OpenAI, Anthropic, Gemini**: API integration experience

---

## ‚ùì Questions to Ask Tyler (HR Recruiter)

### About the Role
1. "What does a typical day look like for this position?"
2. "Who would I be collaborating with most closely? (tech artists, data scientists, game developers?)"
3. ‚≠ê **"What ML/AI projects is the team currently working on or planning?"** (KEY QUESTION)
4. "What AWS services does the team use most heavily?"

### About the Team
5. ‚≠ê **"Can you tell me more about the Marketing Content Production Craft team?"** (KEY QUESTION)
6. "How large is the Fan Growth organization?"
7. "What's the team culture like?"

### About Next Steps
8. "What does the interview process look like after this screen?"
9. "When are you looking to have someone start?"
10. "What's the timeline for next steps?"

### About EA
11. "What makes EA's Fan Growth organization unique compared to other parts of EA?"
12. "How does EA support professional development and learning?"

---

## üö® Red Flags to Avoid

‚ùå **Don't say**:
- Negative things about Amazon or previous employers
- "I don't have experience with X" (reframe as "I haven't used X specifically, but I've used similar tools like Y")
- Appear desperate or over-eager
- Discuss compensation too early (let them bring it up)

‚úÖ **Do say**:
- Specific examples with metrics (82% improvement, 240 dev-hours saved, 40TB/day)
- "That's a great question" (buy yourself thinking time)
- Ask clarifying questions if needed
- Express genuine excitement about EA's mission

---

## üìû Call Logistics Prep

- **Test your setup**: Camera, microphone, internet connection
- **Quiet environment**: No interruptions
- **Have ready**: Resume, JD, this prep guide, notepad
- **Professional background**: Clean, well-lit space
- **Dress code**: Business casual (collared shirt minimum)
- **Join 2-3 minutes early**: Never be late

---

## üéØ Closing Statement

"Thank you for taking the time to speak with me today, Tyler. I'm really excited about this opportunity. The role aligns perfectly with my experience building cloud-native ML applications at Amazon, and I'm particularly drawn to EA's mission of creating engaging experiences for millions of fans. I'm confident I can hit the ground running with AWS, Python, and AI tools to help accelerate the Fan Growth team's product development cycles. I look forward to the next steps!"

---

## üìä Your Match Score: 95%

You are an **excellent match** for this role:
- ‚úÖ 5+ years experience (exceeds 4+ requirement)
- ‚úÖ Python + ML expertise
- ‚úÖ AWS services (all mentioned services)
- ‚úÖ AI tools (Cursor, MCP, n8n)
- ‚úÖ Full-stack development
- ‚úÖ IaC (AWS CDK/CloudFormation)
- ‚úÖ Technical documentation
- ‚úÖ Cross-functional team leadership
- ‚úÖ Hybrid work arrangement compatible

**Confidence level**: HIGH. You have direct experience with every required technology and responsibility.

---

## üéÆ EA Fun Facts (Build Rapport)

- **Franchises**: Apex Legends, Battlefield, EA SPORTS FC, Madden NFL, The Sims
- **Global reach**: Hundreds of millions of players worldwide
- **Fan Growth mission**: "Elevating experiences & maximizing fun"
```

```markdown
# HR Screen Prep Guide - Electronic Arts
## Full Stack Software Engineer - ML Cloud Applications

**Interviewer**: Tyler Poe (HR Recruiter)  
**Company**: Electronic Arts  
**Role**: Full Stack Software Engineer - ML Cloud Applications  
**Team**: Marketing Content Production Craft Team (Fan Growth Organization)

---

## üí° Employment Gap Strategy

**Approach**: Be transparent and authentic
- ‚úÖ **Mention layoff**: "My team and I were laid off in March 2025" (ownership, not personal failure)
- ‚úÖ **Family time**: Spent quality time with family, present for important milestones
- ‚úÖ **Productive learning**: Enrolled in ML program, built full-stack AI applications
- ‚úÖ **Ready & energized**: Expanded skillset, ready to contribute

**Key message**: Turned a challenging situation into an opportunity for growth and family

---

## üéØ Quick Reference - Key Match Points

| **Requirement** | **Your Experience** |
|-----------------|---------------------|
| 4+ years cloud development | ‚úÖ 5+ years at Amazon building AWS cloud-native apps |
| Python + ML proficiency | ‚úÖ Built AI agents, RAG systems, NLP chatbots, ML pipelines |
| AWS services (Lambda, SageMaker, DynamoDB, API Gateway) | ‚úÖ Extensive: Led teams using Lambda, SageMaker, DynamoDB, API Gateway, Step Functions, CDK, CloudWatch |
| AI tools (coding agents, MCP, n8n) | ‚úÖ Heavy user of Cursor, Windsurf, MCP, n8n |
| Full-stack development | ‚úÖ React, TypeScript, Flask, FastAPI, Node.js |
| IaC (CloudFormation) | ‚úÖ AWS CDK & CloudFormation expert, built 4-stage CI/CD pipelines |
| Technical documentation | ‚úÖ Led org-wide documentation workshop at Amazon |
| Cross-functional collaboration | ‚úÖ Led teams of 8 engineers, designers, data scientists |

---

## üìã Common HR Screen Questions & Answers

### 1. "Tell me about yourself"
**Answer (60-90 seconds)**:
"I'm **Aviral Garg**, a software engineer with **5+ years** at **Amazon** building **cloud-native ML applications**. 

I specialize in **full-stack AI-driven solutions** using **AWS services** like **Lambda**, **SageMaker**, **DynamoDB**, and **API Gateway**.

At Amazon, I led a team of **8 engineers** building **serverless data pipelines** processing **40TB/day**, serving **40M+ customers** monthly. 

I also built **internal-documentation-powered AI agents** that improved resolution time by **82%** and saved **240+ dev-hours** per month. Actually reached **100% documentation completion** for the entire team.

Outside Amazon, I've been deeply focused on **AI development**‚Äîbuilding **voice assistants**, **real-time transcription tools**, and **full-stack AI applications**.

I'm excited about EA's role because it combines my passion for **AI/ML**, **cloud architecture**, and creating **engaging experiences** that **millions of people** use."

### 2. "Why are you interested in Electronic Arts?"
**Answer**:
"**Three main reasons**:

**First**, **impact at scale**. EA's games reach **hundreds of millions** of fans globally. I remember hearing "**EA Sports, it's in the game**" since I was a kid. Building **ML-powered cloud applications** that enhance these experiences is incredibly exciting.

**Second**, **technical alignment**. The role perfectly matches my expertise‚Äî**Python**, **AWS** (**Lambda**, **SageMaker**, **DynamoDB**), **AI tools**, **full-stack development**, and **IaC** with **CloudFormation**. I've built exactly these types of systems at Amazon.

**Third**, **innovation and collaboration**. Working with **tech artists**, **data scientists**, **content creators**, and **game developers** to deploy **ML models** and build **automation pipelines**. This aligns with my experience leading **cross-functional teams** and my passion for **AI-driven solutions**."

### 3. "Why are you leaving Amazon?" / "What have you been doing since March?"
**Answer**:
"My **team** and I were **laid off** in **March 2025** as part of **organizational restructuring**. My manager, manager's manager‚Äîwe were all laid off together. Our **Beauty Tech team** was being **merged** into a different team.

After **5+ years** at Amazon, I took that as an opportunity to **take a step back**. I used that time to **work on myself** and spend quality time with **family**. It was a good break.

I also used that time **productively** to deepen my **ML/AI expertise**. I enrolled in a comprehensive **Machine Learning program** covering **EDA**, **Feature Engineering**, **Neural Networks**, **NLP**, and **Agentic Frameworks**.

I built several **full-stack AI applications**‚Äî**voice assistants**, **real-time transcription tools**, and **health misinformation prevention systems**. All leveraging **AWS**, **Python**, and modern **AI tools**.

Now I'm **energized** and ready to bring that expanded skillset to a role like this at EA. I want to build **ML-powered cloud applications** that enhance experiences for **millions of fans**."

### 4. "What's your biggest accomplishment?"
**Answer**:
"At Amazon, I built AI agents powered by internal documentation that answered CI/CD admin questions instantly. This improved resolution time by 82% and projected savings of 240+ dev-hours per month. What made it special was the end-to-end ownership‚ÄîI identified the problem, architected the solution using AWS Lambda and SageMaker, built the RAG pipeline, and drove adoption across the org. It demonstrated my ability to combine ML/AI with cloud infrastructure to solve real business problems‚Äîexactly what this EA role requires."

### 5. "What's your experience with AWS services mentioned in the JD?"
**Answer**:
"Extensive hands-on experience:
- **Lambda & API Gateway**: Built serverless APIs and data pipelines
- **SageMaker**: Deployed ML models (Endpoints, Batch Transform)
- **DynamoDB**: Session persistence, high-throughput data storage
- **CloudWatch & X-Ray**: Built 4-stage CI/CD pipelines with granular monitoring
- **AWS CDK/CloudFormation**: Infrastructure-as-code expert, architected entire deployment pipelines
- **Cognito**: Integrated authentication systems
- **SAM & SSM**: Used for serverless app deployment and parameter management
- **Step Functions**: Orchestrated complex workflows for 40TB/day data processing"

### 6. "What's your experience with AI tools like MCP, n8n, coding agents?"
**Answer**:
"I'm a power user of modern AI development tools:
- **Coding agents**: Daily user of Cursor and Windsurf for AI-assisted development
- **MCP (Model Context Protocol)**: Familiar with the architecture and use cases
- **n8n**: Experience with workflow automation
- **Generative AI platforms**: OpenAI, Anthropic, Gemini, Ollama
- **Real-world application**: Built 'Bob', my personal AI voice assistant with 8 operational modes, reducing platform costs by 40x through prompt engineering

These tools are central to my workflow and I'm excited to leverage them to accelerate EA's product development cycles."

### 7. "How do you handle working with cross-functional teams?"
**Answer**:
"At Amazon, I led teams of 8 engineers, designers, and data scientists. Key practices:
1. **Clear communication**: Led org-wide documentation workshops, ensuring everyone had access to technical reference materials
2. **Stakeholder management**: Collaborated with product managers, data scientists, and external teams
3. **Empowerment**: Enabled team autonomy while maintaining alignment on goals
4. **Documentation**: Created comprehensive technical documentation for every project

This aligns perfectly with the EA role's need to work with tech artists, content creators, data scientists, and game engine programmers."

### 8. "What are your salary expectations?"
**Answer**:
"I'm looking for a competitive package that reflects my 5+ years of experience building cloud-native ML applications at Amazon. I'm open to discussing the full compensation package including base, equity, and benefits. What range does EA typically offer for this role?"

### 9. "What's your availability?"
**Answer**:
"I'm available immediately and flexible with the hybrid arrangement (3 days/week in office). I'm based in Vancouver, BC."

### 10. "Do you have any questions for me?"
**See Questions to Ask section below**

---

## üí° Key Talking Points - Memorize These

### Your AWS Expertise (Match to JD)
- **Lambda**: Serverless API development, event-driven architectures
- **SageMaker**: Model deployment (Endpoints, Batch Transform)
- **DynamoDB**: High-throughput NoSQL database for session persistence
- **API Gateway**: RESTful API development and management
- **CloudWatch & X-Ray**: Monitoring, logging, distributed tracing
- **AWS CDK/CloudFormation**: Infrastructure-as-code, CI/CD pipelines
- **Cognito**: Authentication and authorization
- **SAM & SSM**: Serverless Application Model, Systems Manager
- **Step Functions**: Workflow orchestration

### Your AI/ML Experience (Match to JD)

- Deployed NLP chatbots with full CI/CD
- Integrated OpenAI Whisper for local ML-based speech recognition
- Health misinformation prevention system with multi-agent simulation
- Experience with OpenAI, Anthropic, Gemini, Ollama
- Vector databases, RAG, LLMs, model deployment

### Your Full-Stack Expertise (Match to JD)
```

```markdown
# HR Screen Prep Guide - Electronic Arts
## Full Stack Software Engineer - ML Cloud Applications

**Interviewer**: Tyler Poe (HR Recruiter)  
**Company**: Electronic Arts  
**Role**: Full Stack Software Engineer - ML Cloud Applications  
**Team**: Marketing Content Production Craft Team (Fan Growth Organization)

---

## üí° Employment Gap Strategy

**Approach**: Be transparent and authentic
- ‚úÖ **Mention layoff**: "My team and I were laid off in March 2025" (ownership, not personal failure)
- ‚úÖ **Family time**: Spent quality time with family, present for important milestones
- ‚úÖ **Productive learning**: Enrolled in ML program, built full-stack AI applications
- ‚úÖ **Ready & energized**: Expanded skillset, ready to contribute

**Key message**: Turned a challenging situation into an opportunity for growth and family

---

## üéØ Quick Reference - Key Match Points

| **Requirement** | **Your Experience** |
|-----------------|---------------------|
| 4+ years cloud development | ‚úÖ 5+ years at Amazon building AWS cloud-native apps |
| Python + ML proficiency | ‚úÖ Built AI agents, RAG systems, NLP chatbots, ML pipelines |
| AWS services (Lambda, SageMaker, DynamoDB, API Gateway) | ‚úÖ Extensive: Led teams using Lambda, SageMaker, DynamoDB, API Gateway, Step Functions, CDK, CloudWatch |
| AI tools (coding agents, MCP, n8n) | ‚úÖ Heavy user of Cursor, Windsurf, MCP, n8n |
| Full-stack development | ‚úÖ React, TypeScript, Flask, FastAPI, Node.js |
| IaC (CloudFormation) | ‚úÖ AWS CDK & CloudFormation expert, built 4-stage CI/CD pipelines |
| Technical documentation | ‚úÖ Led org-wide documentation workshop at Amazon |
| Cross-functional collaboration | ‚úÖ Led teams of 8 engineers, designers, data scientists |

---

## üìã Common HR Screen Questions & Answers

### 1. "Tell me about yourself"
**Answer (60-90 seconds)**:
"I'm **Aviral Garg**, a software engineer with **5+ years** at **Amazon** building **cloud-native ML applications**. 

I specialize in **full-stack AI-driven solutions** using **AWS services** like **Lambda**, **SageMaker**, **DynamoDB**, and **API Gateway**.

At Amazon, I led a team of **8 engineers** building **serverless data pipelines** processing **40TB/day**, serving **40M+ customers** monthly. 

I also built **internal-documentation-powered AI agents** that improved resolution time by **82%** and saved **240+ dev-hours** per month. Actually reached **100% documentation completion** for the entire team.

Outside Amazon, I've been deeply focused on **AI development**‚Äîbuilding **voice assistants**, **real-time transcription tools**, and **full-stack AI applications**.

I'm excited about EA's role because it combines my passion for **AI/ML**, **cloud architecture**, and creating **engaging experiences** that **millions of people** use."

### 2. "Why are you interested in Electronic Arts?"
**Answer**:
"**Three main reasons**:

**First**, **impact at scale**. EA's games reach **hundreds of millions** of fans globally. I remember hearing "**EA Sports, it's in the game**" since I was a kid. Building **ML-powered cloud applications** that enhance these experiences is incredibly exciting.

**Second**, **technical alignment**. The role perfectly matches my expertise‚Äî**Python**, **AWS** (**Lambda**, **SageMaker**, **DynamoDB**), **AI tools**, **full-stack development**, and **IaC** with **CloudFormation**. I've built exactly these types of systems at Amazon.

**Third**, **innovation and collaboration**. Working with **tech artists**, **data scientists**, **content creators**, and **game developers** to deploy **ML models** and build **automation pipelines**. This aligns with my experience leading **cross-functional teams** and my passion for **AI-driven solutions**."

### 3. "Why are you leaving Amazon?" / "What have you been doing since March?"
**Answer**:
"My **team** and I were **laid off** in **March 2025** as part of **organizational restructuring**. My manager, manager's manager‚Äîwe were all laid off together. Our **Beauty Tech team** was being **merged** into a different team.

After **5+ years** at Amazon, I took that as an opportunity to **take a step back**. I used that time to **work on myself** and spend quality time with **family**. It was a good break.

I also used that time **productively** to deepen my **ML/AI expertise**. I enrolled in a comprehensive **Machine Learning program** covering **EDA**, **Feature Engineering**, **Neural Networks**, **NLP**, and **Agentic Frameworks**.

I built several **full-stack AI applications**‚Äî**voice assistants**, **real-time transcription tools**, and **health misinformation prevention systems**. All leveraging **AWS**, **Python**, and modern **AI tools**.

Now I'm **energized** and ready to bring that expanded skillset to a role like this at EA. I want to build **ML-powered cloud applications** that enhance experiences for **millions of fans**."

### 4. "What's your biggest accomplishment?"
**Answer**:
"At Amazon, I built **AI agents** powered by **internal documentation** that answered **CI/CD admin questions** instantly. 

This improved **resolution time** by **82%** and projected savings of **240+ dev-hours** per month.

What made it special was the **end-to-end ownership**. I **identified the problem**, **architected the solution** using **AWS Lambda** and **SageMaker**, built the **RAG pipeline**, and drove **adoption** across the org.

It demonstrated my ability to combine **ML/AI** with **cloud infrastructure** to solve **real business problems**‚Äîexactly what this EA role requires."

### 5. "What's your experience with AWS services mentioned in the JD?"
**Answer**:
"**Extensive hands-on experience**:

**Lambda & API Gateway**: Built **serverless APIs** and **data pipelines**

**SageMaker**: Deployed **ML models** (**Endpoints**, **Batch Transform**)

**DynamoDB**: **Session persistence**, **high-throughput** data storage

**CloudWatch & X-Ray**: Built **4-stage CI/CD pipelines** with **granular monitoring**

**AWS CDK/CloudFormation**: **Infrastructure-as-code** expert, architected entire **deployment pipelines**

**Cognito**: Integrated **authentication systems**

**SAM & SSM**: Used for **serverless app deployment** and **parameter management**

**Step Functions**: Orchestrated complex workflows for **40TB/day** data processing"

### 6. "What's your experience with AI tools like MCP, n8n, coding agents?"
**Answer**:
"I'm a power user of modern AI development tools:
- **Coding agents**: Daily user of Cursor and Windsurf for AI-assisted development
- **MCP (Model Context Protocol)**: Familiar with the architecture and use cases
- **n8n**: Experience with workflow automation
- **Generative AI platforms**: OpenAI, Anthropic, Gemini, Ollama
- **Real-world application**: Built 'Bob', my personal AI voice assistant with 8 operational modes, reducing platform costs by 40x through prompt engineering

These tools are central to my workflow and I'm excited to leverage them to accelerate EA's product development cycles."

### 7. "How do you handle working with cross-functional teams?"
**Answer**:
"At Amazon, I led teams of 8 engineers, designers, and data scientists. Key practices:
1. **Clear communication**: Led org-wide documentation workshops, ensuring everyone had access to technical reference materials
2. **Stakeholder management**: Collaborated with product managers, data scientists, and external teams
3. **Empowerment**: Enabled team autonomy while maintaining alignment on goals
4. **Documentation**: Created comprehensive technical documentation for every project

This aligns perfectly with the EA role's need to work with tech artists, content creators, data scientists, and game engine programmers."

### 8. "What are your salary expectations?"
**Answer**:
"I'm looking for a competitive package that reflects my 5+ years of experience building cloud-native ML applications at Amazon. I'm open to discussing the full compensation package including base, equity, and benefits. What range does EA typically offer for this role?"

### 9. "What's your availability?"
**Answer**:
"I'm available immediately and flexible with the hybrid arrangement (3 days/week in office). I'm based in Vancouver, BC."

### 10. "Do you have any questions for me?"
**See Questions to Ask section below**

---

## üí° Key Talking Points - Memorize These

### Your AWS Expertise (Match to JD)
- **Lambda**: Serverless API development, event-driven architectures
- **SageMaker**: Model deployment (Endpoints, Batch Transform)
- **DynamoDB**: High-throughput NoSQL database for session persistence
- **API Gateway**: RESTful API development and management
- **CloudWatch & X-Ray**: Monitoring, logging, distributed tracing
- **AWS CDK/CloudFormation**: Infrastructure-as-code, CI/CD pipelines
- **Cognito**: Authentication and authorization
- **SAM & SSM**: Serverless Application Model, Systems Manager
- **Step Functions**: Workflow orchestration

### Your AI/ML Experience (Match to JD)
- Built AI agents for documentation Q&A (RAG pipeline)
- Deployed NLP chatbots with full CI/CD
- Integrated OpenAI Whisper for local ML-based speech recognition
- Health misinformation prevention system with multi-agent simulation
- Experience with OpenAI, Anthropic, Gemini, Ollama
- Vector databases, RAG, LLMs, model deployment

### Your Full-Stack Expertise (Match to JD)
- **Frontend**: React 19, TypeScript
- **Backend**: Python (Flask, FastAPI), Node.js
- **Databases**: DynamoDB, PostgreSQL, SQLite
- **APIs**: RESTful API design and implementation
- **CI/CD**: GitHub Actions, AWS CDK pipelines
- **IaC**: AWS CDK, CloudFormation

### Your Documentation & Collaboration (Match to JD)
- Led org-wide documentation workshop at Amazon
- "Robust documentation & operational readiness" recognition
- Led teams of 8 engineers, designers, data scientists
- Cross-functional collaboration with multiple teams

### Your AI Development Tools (Match to JD)
- **Coding agents**: Cursor, Windsurf (daily use)
- **MCP**: Model Context Protocol familiarity
- **n8n**: Workflow automation
- **OpenAI, Anthropic, Gemini**: API integration experience

---

## ‚ùì Questions to Ask Tyler (HR Recruiter)

### About the Role
1. "What does a typical day look like for this position?"
2. "Who would I be collaborating with most closely? (tech artists, data scientists, game developers?)"
3. ‚≠ê **"What ML/AI projects is the team currently working on or planning?"** (KEY QUESTION)
4. "What AWS services does the team use most heavily?"

### About the Team
5. ‚≠ê **"Can you tell me more about the Marketing Content Production Craft team?"** (KEY QUESTION)
6. "How large is the Fan Growth organization?"
7. "What's the team culture like?"

### About Next Steps
8. "What does the interview process look like after this screen?"
9. "When are you looking to have someone start?"
10. "What's the timeline for next steps?"

### About EA
11. "What makes EA's Fan Growth organization unique compared to other parts of EA?"
12. "How does EA support professional development and learning?"

---

## üö® Red Flags to Avoid

‚ùå **Don't say**:
- Negative things about Amazon or previous employers
- "I don't have experience with X" (reframe as "I haven't used X specifically, but I've used similar tools like Y")
- Appear desperate or over-eager
- Discuss compensation too early (let them bring it up)

‚úÖ **Do say**:
- Specific examples with metrics (82% improvement, 240 dev-hours saved, 40TB/day)
- "That's a great question" (buy yourself thinking time)
- Ask clarifying questions if needed
- Express genuine excitement about EA's mission

---

- **Quiet environment**: No interruptions
- **Have ready**: Resume, JD, this prep guide, notepad
- **Professional background**: Clean, well-lit space
- **Dress code**: Business casual (collared shirt minimum)
- **Join 2-3 minutes early**: Never be late

"Thank you for taking the time to speak with me today, Tyler. I'm really excited about this opportunity. The role aligns perfectly with my experience building cloud-native ML applications at Amazon, and I'm particularly drawn to EA's mission of creating engaging experiences for millions of fans. I'm confident I can hit the ground running with AWS, Python, and AI tools to help accelerate the Fan Growth team's product development cycles. I look forward to the next steps!"
```

```markdown
"I'm **Aviral Garg**, a software engineer with **5+ years** at **Amazon** building **cloud-native ML applications**.
```

```markdown
At Amazon, I led a team of **8 engineers** building **serverless data pipelines** processing **40TB/day**, serving **40M+ customers** monthly. 

I also built **internal-documentation-powered AI agents** that improved resolution time by **82%** and saved **240+ dev-hours** per month. Actually reached **100% documentation completion** for the entire team.

Outside Amazon, I've been deeply focused on **AI development**‚Äîbuilding **voice assistants**, **real-time transcription tools**, and **full-stack AI applications**.

I'm excited about EA's role because it combines my passion for **AI/ML**, **cloud architecture**, and creating **engaging experiences** that **millions of people** use."

### 2. "Why are you interested in Electronic Arts?"
**Answer**:
"**Three main reasons**:

**First**, **impact at scale**. EA's games reach **hundreds of millions** of fans globally. I remember hearing "**EA Sports, it's in the game**" since I was a kid. Building **ML-powered cloud applications** that enhance these experiences is incredibly exciting.

**Second**, **technical alignment**. The role perfectly matches my expertise‚Äî**Python**, **AWS** (**Lambda**, **SageMaker**, **DynamoDB**), **AI tools**, **full-stack development**, and **IaC** with **CloudFormation**. I've built exactly these types of systems at Amazon.

**Third**, **innovation and collaboration**. Working with **tech artists**, **data scientists**, **content creators**, and **game developers** to deploy **ML models** and build **automation pipelines**. This aligns with my experience leading **cross-functional teams** and my passion for **AI-driven solutions**."

### 3. "Why are you leaving Amazon?" / "What have you been doing since March?"
**Answer**:
"My **team** and I were **laid off** in **March 2025** as part of **organizational restructuring**. My manager, manager's manager‚Äîwe were all laid off together. Our **Beauty Tech team** was being **merged** into a different team.

After **5+ years** at Amazon, I took that as an opportunity to **take a step back**. I used that time to **work on myself** and spend quality time with **family**. It was a good break.

I also used that time **productively** to deepen my **ML/AI expertise**. I enrolled in a comprehensive **Machine Learning program** covering **EDA**, **Feature Engineering**, **Neural Networks**, **NLP**, and **Agentic Frameworks**.

I built several **full-stack AI applications**‚Äî**voice assistants**, **real-time transcription tools**, and **health misinformation prevention systems**. All leveraging **AWS**, **Python**, and modern **AI tools**.

Now I'm **energized** and ready to bring that expanded skillset to a role like this at EA. I want to build **ML-powered cloud applications** that enhance experiences for **millions of fans**."

### 4. "What's your biggest accomplishment?"
**Answer**:
"At Amazon, I built **AI agents** powered by **internal documentation** that answered **CI/CD admin questions** instantly. 

This improved **resolution time** by **82%** and projected savings of **240+ dev-hours** per month.

What made it special was the **end-to-end ownership**. I **identified the problem**, **architected the solution** using **AWS Lambda** and **SageMaker**, built the **RAG pipeline**, and drove **adoption** across the org.

It demonstrated my ability to combine **ML/AI** with **cloud infrastructure** to solve **real business problems**‚Äîexactly what this EA role requires."

### 5. "What's your experience with AWS services mentioned in the JD?"
**Answer**:
"**Extensive hands-on experience**:

**Lambda & API Gateway**: Built **serverless APIs** and **data pipelines**

**SageMaker**: Deployed **ML models** (**Endpoints**, **Batch Transform**)

**DynamoDB**: **Session persistence**, **high-throughput** data storage

**CloudWatch & X-Ray**: Built **4-stage CI/CD pipelines** with **granular monitoring**

**AWS CDK/CloudFormation**: **Infrastructure-as-code** expert, architected entire **deployment pipelines**

**Cognito**: Integrated **authentication systems**

**SAM & SSM**: Used for **serverless app deployment** and **parameter management**

**Step Functions**: Orchestrated complex workflows for **40TB/day** data processing"

### 6. "What's your experience with AI tools like MCP, n8n, coding agents?"
**Answer**:
"I'm a **power user** of modern **AI development tools**:

**Coding agents**: Daily user of **Cursor** and **Windsurf** for **AI-assisted development**

**MCP** (Model Context Protocol): Familiar with the **architecture** and **use cases**

**n8n**: Experience with **workflow automation**

**Generative AI platforms**: **OpenAI**, **Anthropic**, **Gemini**, **Ollama**

**Real-world application**: Built **'Bob'**, my personal **AI voice assistant** with **8 operational modes**. Reduced platform costs by **40x** through **prompt engineering**.

These tools are central to my workflow. I'm excited to leverage them to **accelerate EA's product development cycles**."

### 7. "How do you handle working with cross-functional teams?"
**Answer**:
"At Amazon, I led teams of **8 engineers**, **designers**, and **data scientists**. 

**Key practices**:

**Clear communication**: Led **org-wide documentation workshops**, ensuring everyone had access to **technical reference materials**

**Stakeholder management**: Collaborated with **product managers**, **data scientists**, and **external teams**

**Empowerment**: Enabled **team autonomy** while maintaining **alignment** on goals

**Documentation**: Created **comprehensive technical documentation** for every project

This aligns perfectly with the EA role's need to work with **tech artists**, **content creators**, **data scientists**, and **game engine programmers**."

### 8. "What are your salary expectations?"
**Answer**:
"I'm looking for a competitive package that reflects my 5+ years of experience building cloud-native ML applications at Amazon. I'm open to discussing the full compensation package including base, equity, and benefits. What range does EA typically offer for this role?"

### 9. "What's your availability?"
**Answer**:
"I'm available immediately and flexible with the hybrid arrangement (3 days/week in office). I'm based in Vancouver, BC."

### 10. "Do you have any questions for me?"
**See Questions to Ask section below**

---

## üí° Key Talking Points - Memorize These

### Your AWS Expertise (Match to JD)
- **Lambda**: Serverless API development, event-driven architectures
- **SageMaker**: Model deployment (Endpoints, Batch Transform)
- **DynamoDB**: High-throughput NoSQL database for session persistence
- **API Gateway**: RESTful API development and management
- **CloudWatch & X-Ray**: Monitoring, logging, distributed tracing
- **AWS CDK/CloudFormation**: Infrastructure-as-code, CI/CD pipelines
- **Cognito**: Authentication and authorization
- **SAM & SSM**: Serverless Application Model, Systems Manager
- **Step Functions**: Workflow orchestration

### Your AI/ML Experience (Match to JD)
- Built AI agents for documentation Q&A (RAG pipeline)
- Deployed NLP chatbots with full CI/CD
- Integrated OpenAI Whisper for local ML-based speech recognition
- Health misinformation prevention system with multi-agent simulation
- Experience with OpenAI, Anthropic, Gemini, Ollama
- Vector databases, RAG, LLMs, model deployment

### Your Full-Stack Expertise (Match to JD)
- **Frontend**: React 19, TypeScript
- **Backend**: Python (Flask, FastAPI), Node.js
- **Databases**: DynamoDB, PostgreSQL, SQLite
- **APIs**: RESTful API design and implementation
- **CI/CD**: GitHub Actions, AWS CDK pipelines
- **IaC**: AWS CDK, CloudFormation

### Your Documentation & Collaboration (Match to JD)
- Led org-wide documentation workshop at Amazon
- "Robust documentation & operational readiness" recognition
- Led teams of 8 engineers, designers, data scientists
- Cross-functional collaboration with multiple teams

### Your AI Development Tools (Match to JD)
- **Coding agents**: Cursor, Windsurf (daily use)
- **MCP**: Model Context Protocol familiarity
- **n8n**: Workflow automation
- **OpenAI, Anthropic, Gemini**: API integration experience

---

## ‚ùì Questions to Ask Tyler (HR Recruiter)

### About the Role
1. "What does a typical day look like for this position?"
2. "Who would I be collaborating with most closely? (tech artists, data scientists, game developers?)"
3. ‚≠ê **"What ML/AI projects is the team currently working on or planning?"** (KEY QUESTION)
4. "What AWS services does the team use most heavily?"

### About the Team
5. ‚≠ê **"Can you tell me more about the Marketing Content Production Craft team?"** (KEY QUESTION)
6. "How large is the Fan Growth organization?"
7. "What's the team culture like?"

### About Next Steps
8. "What does the interview process look like after this screen?"
9. "When are you looking to have someone start?"
10. "What's the timeline for next steps?"

### About EA
11. "What makes EA's Fan Growth organization unique compared to other parts of EA?"
12. "How does EA support professional development and learning?"

---

## üö® Red Flags to Avoid

‚ùå **Don't say**:
- Negative things about Amazon or previous employers
- "I don't have experience with X" (reframe as "I haven't used X specifically, but I've used similar tools like Y")
- Appear desperate or over-eager
- Discuss compensation too early (let them bring it up)

‚úÖ **Do say**:
- Specific examples with metrics (82% improvement, 240 dev-hours saved, 40TB/day)
- "That's a great question" (buy yourself thinking time)
- Ask clarifying questions if needed
- Express genuine excitement about EA's mission

---

## üìû Call Logistics Prep

- **Test your setup**: Camera, microphone, internet connection
- **Quiet environment**: No interruptions
- **Have ready**: Resume, JD, this prep guide, notepad
- **Professional background**: Clean, well-lit space
- **Dress code**: Business casual (collared shirt minimum)
- **Join 2-3 minutes early**: Never be late

---

## üéØ Closing Statement

"Thank you for taking the time to speak with me today, Tyler. I'm really excited about this opportunity. The role aligns perfectly with my experience building cloud-native ML applications at Amazon, and I'm particularly drawn to EA's mission of creating engaging experiences for millions of fans. I'm confident I can hit the ground running with AWS, Python, and AI tools to help accelerate the Fan Growth team's product development cycles. I look forward to the next steps!"

---

## üìä Your Match Score: 95%

You are an **excellent match** for this role:
- ‚úÖ 5+ years experience (exceeds 4+ requirement)
- ‚úÖ Python + ML expertise
- ‚úÖ AWS services (all mentioned services)
- ‚úÖ AI tools (Cursor, MCP, n8n)
- ‚úÖ Full-stack development
- ‚úÖ IaC (AWS CDK/CloudFormation)
- ‚úÖ Technical documentation
- ‚úÖ Cross-functional team leadership
- ‚úÖ Hybrid work arrangement compatible

**Confidence level**: HIGH. You have direct experience with every required technology and responsibility.

---

## üéÆ EA Fun Facts (Build Rapport)

- **Franchises**: Apex Legends, Battlefield, EA SPORTS FC, Madden NFL, The Sims
- **Global reach**: Hundreds of millions of players worldwide
- **Fan Growth mission**: "Elevating experiences & maximizing fun"
- **Culture**: "Show up excited to work and ready for fun", celebrates inclusion
- **Perks**: Free games! (mention if it comes up naturally)

---

**Good luck with your HR screen! You've got this! üöÄ**
```

```markdown
# HR Screen Prep Guide - Electronic Arts
## Full Stack Software Engineer - ML Cloud Applications

**Interviewer**: Tyler Poe (HR Recruiter)  
**Company**: Electronic Arts  
**Role**: Full Stack Software Engineer - ML Cloud Applications  
**Team**: Marketing Content Production Craft Team (Fan Growth Organization)

**Approach**: Be transparent and authentic
- ‚úÖ **Mention layoff**: "My team and I were laid off in March 2025" (ownership, not personal failure)
- ‚úÖ **Family time**: Spent quality time with family, present for important milestones
- ‚úÖ **Productive learning**: Enrolled in ML program, built full-stack AI applications
- ‚úÖ **Ready & energized**: Expanded skillset, ready to contribute

**Key message**: Turned a challenging situation into an opportunity for growth and family

---

|-----------------|---------------------|
| 4+ years cloud development | ‚úÖ 5+ years at Amazon building AWS cloud-native apps |
| Python + ML proficiency | ‚úÖ Built AI agents, RAG systems, NLP chatbots, ML pipelines |
| AWS services (Lambda, SageMaker, DynamoDB, API Gateway) | ‚úÖ Extensive: Led teams using Lambda, SageMaker, DynamoDB, API Gateway, Step Functions, CDK, CloudWatch |
| AI tools (coding agents, MCP, n8n) | ‚úÖ Heavy user of Cursor, Windsurf, MCP, n8n |
| Full-stack development | ‚úÖ React, TypeScript, Flask, FastAPI, Node.js |
| IaC (CloudFormation) | ‚úÖ AWS CDK & CloudFormation expert, built 4-stage CI/CD pipelines |
| Technical documentation | ‚úÖ Led org-wide documentation workshop at Amazon |
| Cross-functional collaboration | ‚úÖ Led teams of 8 engineers, designers, data scientists |

"At Amazon, I built **AI agents** powered by **internal documentation** that answered **CI/CD admin questions** instantly. 

This improved **resolution time** by **82%** and projected savings of **240+ dev-hours** per month.

What made it special was the **end-to-end ownership**. I **identified the problem**, **architected the solution** using **AWS Lambda** and **SageMaker**, built the **RAG pipeline**, and drove **adoption** across the org.

It demonstrated my ability to combine **ML/AI** with **cloud infrastructure** to solve **real business problems**‚Äîexactly what this EA role requires."

### 5. "What's your experience with AWS services mentioned in the JD?"
**Answer**:
"**Extensive hands-on experience**:

**Lambda & API Gateway**: Built **serverless APIs** and **data pipelines**

**SageMaker**: Deployed **ML models** (**Endpoints**, **Batch Transform**)

**DynamoDB**: **Session persistence**, **high-throughput** data storage

**CloudWatch & X-Ray**: Built **4-stage CI/CD pipelines** with **granular monitoring**

**AWS CDK/CloudFormation**: **Infrastructure-as-code** expert, architected entire **deployment pipelines**

**Cognito**: Integrated **authentication systems**

**SAM & SSM**: Used for **serverless app deployment** and **parameter management**

**Step Functions**: Orchestrated complex workflows for **40TB/day** data processing"

### 6. "What's your experience with AI tools like MCP, n8n, coding agents?"
**Answer**:
"I'm a **power user** of modern **AI development tools**:

**Coding agents**: Daily user of **Cursor** and **Windsurf** for **AI-assisted development**

**MCP** (Model Context Protocol): Familiar with the **architecture** and **use cases**

**n8n**: Experience with **workflow automation**

**Generative AI platforms**: **OpenAI**, **Anthropic**, **Gemini**, **Ollama**

**Real-world application**: Built **'Bob'**, my personal **AI voice assistant** with **8 operational modes**. Reduced platform costs by **40x** through **prompt engineering**.

These tools are central to my workflow. I'm excited to leverage them to **accelerate EA's product development cycles**."

### 7. "How do you handle working with cross-functional teams?"
**Answer**:
"At Amazon, I led teams of **8 engineers**, **designers**, and **data scientists**. 

**Key practices**:

**Clear communication**: Led **org-wide documentation workshops**, ensuring everyone had access to **technical reference materials**

**Stakeholder management**: Collaborated with **product managers**, **data scientists**, and **external teams**

**Empowerment**: Enabled **team autonomy** while maintaining **alignment** on goals

**Documentation**: Created **comprehensive technical documentation** for every project

This aligns perfectly with the EA role's need to work with **tech artists**, **content creators**, **data scientists**, and **game engine programmers**."

### 8. "What are your salary expectations?"
**Answer**:
"I'm looking for a **competitive package** that reflects my **5+ years** of experience building **cloud-native ML applications** at Amazon. 

I'm open to discussing the **full compensation package** including **base**, **equity**, and **benefits**. 

What range does EA typically offer for this role?"

### 9. "What's your availability?"
**Answer**:
"I'm **available immediately** and flexible with the **hybrid arrangement** (**3 days/week in office**). 

I'm based in **Vancouver, BC**."

### 10. "Do you have any questions for me?"
**See Questions to Ask section below**
```

```markdown
# HR Screen Prep Guide - Electronic Arts
## Full Stack Software Engineer - ML Cloud Applications

**Interviewer**: Tyler Poe (HR Recruiter)  
**Company**: Electronic Arts  
**Role**: Full Stack Software Engineer - ML Cloud Applications  
**Team**: Marketing Content Production Craft Team (Fan Growth Organization)

## üí° Employment Gap Strategy

**Approach**: Be transparent and authentic
- ‚úÖ **Mention layoff**: "My team and I were laid off in March 2025" (ownership, not personal failure)
- ‚úÖ **Family time**: Spent quality time with family, present for important milestones
- ‚úÖ **Productive learning**: Enrolled in ML program, built full-stack AI applications
- ‚úÖ **Ready & energized**: Expanded skillset, ready to contribute

**Key message**: Turned a challenging situation into an opportunity for growth and family

---

| **Requirement** | **Your Experience** |
|-----------------|---------------------|
| 4+ years cloud development | ‚úÖ 5+ years at Amazon building AWS cloud-native apps |

| AWS services (Lambda, SageMaker, DynamoDB, API Gateway) | ‚úÖ Extensive: Led teams using Lambda, SageMaker, DynamoDB, API Gateway, Step Functions, CDK, CloudWatch |
| AI tools (coding agents, MCP, n8n) | ‚úÖ Heavy user of Cursor, Windsurf, MCP, n8n |
| Full-stack development | ‚úÖ React, TypeScript, Flask, FastAPI, Node.js |
| IaC (CloudFormation) | ‚úÖ AWS CDK & CloudFormation expert, built 4-stage CI/CD pipelines |
| Technical documentation | ‚úÖ Led org-wide documentation workshop at Amazon |
| Cross-functional collaboration | ‚úÖ Led teams of 8 engineers, designers, data scientists |
```
