## üìã Common HR Screen Questions & Answers

### 1. "Tell me about yourself"
**Answer (60-90 seconds)**:
"I'm **Aviral Garg**. **5+ years** at **Amazon** building **cloud-native ML applications**. 

Specialize in **full-stack AI solutions** using **AWS**‚Äî**Lambda**, **SageMaker**, **DynamoDB**, **API Gateway**.

At Amazon: Led **8 engineers** building **serverless pipelines** processing **40TB/day**, serving **40M+ customers** monthly. 

Built **AI agents** that improved resolution time by **82%**, saved **240+ dev-hours/month**, reached **100% documentation completion**.

Recent focus: **AI development**‚Äî**voice assistants**, **real-time transcription**, **full-stack AI apps**.

Excited about EA because it combines **AI/ML**, **cloud architecture**, and creating experiences for **millions of fans**."

### 2. "Why are you interested in Electronic Arts?"
**Answer**:
"**Three main reasons**:

**First**, **impact at scale**. EA's games reach **hundreds of millions** of fans globally. I remember hearing "**EA Sports, it's in the game**" since I was a kid. Building **ML-powered cloud applications** that enhance these experiences is incredibly exciting.

**Second**, **technical alignment**. The role perfectly matches my expertise‚Äî**Python**, **AWS** (**Lambda**, **SageMaker**, **DynamoDB**), **AI tools**, **full-stack development**, and **IaC** with **CloudFormation**. I've built exactly these types of systems at Amazon.

**Third**, **innovation and collaboration**. Working with **tech artists**, **data scientists**, **content creators**, and **game developers** to deploy **ML models** and build **automation pipelines**. This aligns with my experience leading **cross-functional teams** and my passion for **AI-driven solutions**."

### 3. "Why are you leaving Amazon?" / "What have you been doing since March?"
**Answer**:
"My **team** and I were **laid off** in **March 2025** as part of **organizational restructuring**. My manager, manager's manager‚Äîwe were all laid off together. Our **Beauty Tech team** was being **merged** into a different team.

After **5+ years** at Amazon, I took that as an opportunity to **take a step back**. I used that time to **work on myself** and spend quality time with **family**. It was a good break.

I also used that time **productively** to deepen my **ML/AI expertise**. I enrolled in a comprehensive **Machine Learning program** covering **EDA**, **Feature Engineering**, **Neural Networks**, **NLP**, and **Agentic Frameworks**.

I built several **full-stack AI applications**‚Äî**voice assistants**, **real-time transcription tools**, and **health misinformation prevention systems**. All leveraging **AWS**, **Python**, and modern **AI tools**.

Now I'm **energized** and ready to bring that expanded skillset to a role like this at EA. I want to build **ML-powered cloud applications** that enhance experiences for **millions of fans**."

### 4. "What's your biggest accomplishment?"
**Answer**:
"At Amazon, I built **AI agents** powered by **internal documentation** that answered **CI/CD admin questions** instantly. 

This improved **resolution time** by **82%** and projected savings of **240+ dev-hours** per month.

What made it special was the **end-to-end ownership**. I **identified the problem**, **architected the solution** using **AWS Lambda** and **SageMaker**, built the **RAG pipeline**, and drove **adoption** across the org.

It demonstrated my ability to combine **ML/AI** with **cloud infrastructure** to solve **real business problems**‚Äîexactly what this EA role requires."

### 5. "What's your experience with AWS services mentioned in the JD?"
**Answer**:
"**Extensive hands-on experience**:

**Lambda & API Gateway**: Built **serverless APIs** and **data pipelines**

**SageMaker**: Deployed **ML models** (**Endpoints**, **Batch Transform**)

**DynamoDB**: **Session persistence**, **high-throughput** data storage

**CloudWatch & X-Ray**: Built **4-stage CI/CD pipelines** with **granular monitoring**

**AWS CDK/CloudFormation**: **Infrastructure-as-code** expert, architected entire **deployment pipelines**

**Cognito**: Integrated **authentication systems**

**SAM & SSM**: Used for **serverless app deployment** and **parameter management**

**Step Functions**: Orchestrated complex workflows for **40TB/day** data processing"

### 6. "What's your experience with AI tools like MCP, n8n, coding agents?"
**Answer**:
"I'm a **power user** of modern **AI development tools**:

**Coding agents**: Daily user of **Cursor** and **Windsurf** for **AI-assisted development**

**MCP** (Model Context Protocol): Familiar with the **architecture** and **use cases**

**n8n**: Experience with **workflow automation**

**Generative AI platforms**: **OpenAI**, **Anthropic**, **Gemini**, **Ollama**

**Real-world application**: Built **'Bob'**, my personal **AI voice assistant** with **8 operational modes**. Reduced platform costs by **40x** through **prompt engineering**.

These tools are central to my workflow. I'm excited to leverage them to **accelerate EA's product development cycles**."

### 7. "How do you handle working with cross-functional teams?"
**Answer**:

**n8n**: Experience with **workflow automation**

**Generative AI platforms**: **OpenAI**, **Anthropic**, **Gemini**, **Ollama**

**Real-world application**: Built **'Bob'**, my personal **AI voice assistant** with **8 operational modes**. Reduced platform costs by **40x** through **prompt engineering**.

These tools are central to my workflow. I'm excited to leverage them to **accelerate EA's product development cycles**."

### 7. "How do you handle working with cross-functional teams?"
**Answer**:
"At Amazon, I led teams of **8 engineers**, **designers**, and **data scientists**. 

**Key practices**:

**Clear communication**: Led **org-wide documentation workshops**, ensuring everyone had access to **technical reference materials**

**Stakeholder management**: Collaborated with **product managers**, **data scientists**, and **external teams**

**Empowerment**: Enabled **team autonomy** while maintaining **alignment** on goals

**Documentation**: Created **comprehensive technical documentation** for every project

This aligns perfectly with the EA role's need to work with **tech artists**, **content creators**, **data scientists**, and **game engine programmers**."

### 8. "What are your salary expectations?"
**Answer**:
"I'm looking for a **competitive package** that reflects my **5+ years** of experience building **cloud-native ML applications** at Amazon. 

I'm open to discussing the **full compensation package** including **base**, **equity**, and **benefits**. 

What range does EA typically offer for this role?"

### 9. "What's your availability?"
**Answer**:
"I'm **available immediately** and flexible with the **hybrid arrangement** (**3 days/week in office**). 

I'm based in **Vancouver, BC**."

### 10. "Do you have any questions for me?"
**See Questions to Ask section below**

---

## üí° Key Talking Points - Memorize These

### Your AWS Expertise (Match to JD)
- **Lambda**: Serverless API development, event-driven architectures
- **SageMaker**: Model deployment (Endpoints, Batch Transform)
- **DynamoDB**: High-throughput NoSQL database for session persistence
- **API Gateway**: RESTful API development and management
- **CloudWatch & X-Ray**: Monitoring, logging, distributed tracing
- **AWS CDK/CloudFormation**: Infrastructure-as-code, CI/CD pipelines
- **Cognito**: Authentication and authorization
- **SAM & SSM**: Serverless Application Model, Systems Manager
- **Step Functions**: Workflow orchestration

### Your AI/ML Experience (Match to JD)
- Built AI agents for documentation Q&A (RAG pipeline)
- Deployed NLP chatbots with full CI/CD
- Integrated OpenAI Whisper for local ML-based speech recognition
- Health misinformation prevention system with multi-agent simulation
- Experience with OpenAI, Anthropic, Gemini, Ollama
- Vector databases, RAG, LLMs, model deployment

### Your Full-Stack Expertise (Match to JD)
- **Frontend**: React 19, TypeScript
- **Backend**: Python (Flask, FastAPI), Node.js
- **Databases**: DynamoDB, PostgreSQL, SQLite
- **APIs**: RESTful API design and implementation
- **CI/CD**: GitHub Actions, AWS CDK pipelines
- **IaC**: AWS CDK, CloudFormation

### Your Documentation & Collaboration (Match to JD)
- Led org-wide documentation workshop at Amazon
- "Robust documentation & operational readiness" recognition
- Led teams of 8 engineers, designers, data scientists
- Cross-functional collaboration with multiple teams

### Your AI Development Tools (Match to JD)
- **Coding agents**: Cursor, Windsurf (daily use)
- **MCP**: Model Context Protocol familiarity
- **n8n**: Workflow automation
- **OpenAI, Anthropic, Gemini**: API integration experience

---

## ‚ùì Questions to Ask Tyler (HR Recruiter)

### About the Role
1. "What does a typical day look like for this position?"
2. "Who would I be collaborating with most closely? (tech artists, data scientists, game developers?)"
3. ‚≠ê **"What ML/AI projects is the team currently working on or planning?"** (KEY QUESTION)
4. "What AWS services does the team use most heavily?"

### About the Team
5. ‚≠ê **"Can you tell me more about the Marketing Content Production Craft team?"** (KEY QUESTION)

7. "What's the team culture like?"

### About Next Steps

10. "What's the timeline for next steps?"

### About EA
11. "What makes EA's Fan Growth organization unique compared to other parts of EA?"
12. "How does EA support professional development and learning?"

---

## üö® Red Flags to Avoid

‚ùå **Don't say**:
- Negative things about Amazon or previous employers
- "I don't have experience with X" (reframe as "I haven't used X specifically, but I've used similar tools like Y")
- Appear desperate or over-eager
- Discuss compensation too early (let them bring it up)

‚úÖ **Do say**:
- Specific examples with metrics (82% improvement, 240 dev-hours saved, 40TB/day)
- "That's a great question" (buy yourself thinking time)
- Ask clarifying questions if needed
- Express genuine excitement about EA's mission

---

- **Test your setup**: Camera, microphone, internet connection
- **Quiet environment**: No interruptions
- **Have ready**: Resume, JD, this prep guide, notepad
- **Professional background**: Clean, well-lit space
- **Dress code**: Business casual (collared shirt minimum)
- **Join 2-3 minutes early**: Never be late

---

## üéØ Closing Statement

"Thank you for taking the time to speak with me today, **Tyler**. I'm really **excited** about this opportunity. 

The role aligns **perfectly** with my experience building **cloud-native ML applications** at Amazon. I'm particularly drawn to **EA's mission** of creating **engaging experiences** for **millions of fans**. 

I'm confident I can **hit the ground running** with **AWS**, **Python**, and **AI tools** to help accelerate the **Fan Growth team's product development cycles**. 

I look forward to the **next steps**!"

---

## üìä Your Match Score: 95%

You are an **excellent match** for this role:
- ‚úÖ 5+ years experience (exceeds 4+ requirement)
- ‚úÖ Python + ML expertise
- ‚úÖ AWS services (all mentioned services)
- ‚úÖ AI tools (Cursor, MCP, n8n)
- ‚úÖ Full-stack development
- ‚úÖ IaC (AWS CDK/CloudFormation)
- ‚úÖ Technical documentation
- ‚úÖ Cross-functional team leadership
- ‚úÖ Hybrid work arrangement compatible

**Confidence level**: HIGH. You have direct experience with every required technology and responsibility.

---

## üéÆ EA Fun Facts (Build Rapport)

- **Franchises**: Apex Legends, Battlefield, EA SPORTS FC, Madden NFL, The Sims
- **Global reach**: Hundreds of millions of players worldwide
- **Fan Growth mission**: "Elevating experiences & maximizing fun"
- **Culture**: "Show up excited to work and ready for fun", celebrates inclusion
- **Perks**: Free games! (mention if it comes up naturally)

# HR Screen Prep Guide - Electronic Arts
## Full Stack Software Engineer - ML Cloud Applications

**Interviewer**: Tyler Poe (HR Recruiter)  
**Company**: Electronic Arts  
**Role**: Full Stack Software Engineer - ML Cloud Applications  
**Team**: Marketing Content Production Craft Team (Fan Growth Organization)

---

## üí° Employment Gap Strategy

**Approach**: Be transparent and authentic
- ‚úÖ **Mention layoff**: "My team and I were laid off in March 2025" (ownership, not personal failure)
- ‚úÖ **Family time**: Spent quality time with family, present for important milestones
- ‚úÖ **Productive learning**: Enrolled in ML program, built full-stack AI applications
- ‚úÖ **Ready & energized**: Expanded skillset, ready to contribute

**Key message**: Turned a challenging situation into an opportunity for growth and family

---

## üéØ Quick Reference - Key Match Points

| **Requirement** | **Your Experience** |
|-----------------|---------------------|
| 4+ years cloud development | ‚úÖ 5+ years at Amazon building AWS cloud-native apps |
| Python + ML proficiency | ‚úÖ Built AI agents, RAG systems, NLP chatbots, ML pipelines |
| AWS services (Lambda, SageMaker, DynamoDB, API Gateway) | ‚úÖ Extensive: Led teams using Lambda, SageMaker, DynamoDB, API Gateway, Step Functions, CDK, CloudWatch |
| AI tools (coding agents, MCP, n8n) | ‚úÖ Heavy user of Cursor, Windsurf, MCP, n8n |
| Full-stack development | ‚úÖ React, TypeScript, Flask, FastAPI, Node.js |
| IaC (CloudFormation) | ‚úÖ AWS CDK & CloudFormation expert, built 4-stage CI/CD pipelines |
| Technical documentation | ‚úÖ Led org-wide documentation workshop at Amazon |
| Cross-functional collaboration | ‚úÖ Led teams of 8 engineers, designers, data scientists |

---

## üìã Common HR Screen Questions & Answers

### 1. "Tell me about yourself"
**Answer (60-90 seconds)**:
"I'm **Aviral Garg**. **5+ years** at **Amazon** building **cloud-native ML applications**. 

Specialize in **full-stack AI solutions** using **AWS**‚Äî**Lambda**, **SageMaker**, **DynamoDB**, **API Gateway**.

At Amazon: Led **8 engineers** building **serverless pipelines** processing **40TB/day**, serving **40M+ customers** monthly. 

Built **AI agents** that improved resolution time by **82%**, saved **240+ dev-hours/month**, reached **100% documentation completion**.

Recent focus: **AI development**‚Äî**voice assistants**, **real-time transcription**, **full-stack AI apps**.

Excited about EA because it combines **AI/ML**, **cloud architecture**, and creating experiences for **millions of fans**."

### 2. "Why are you interested in Electronic Arts?"
**Answer**:
"**Three reasons**:

**First**, **impact at scale**. EA's games reach **hundreds of millions** globally. Grew up hearing "**EA Sports, it's in the game**". Building **ML cloud apps** that enhance these experiences is exciting.

**Second**, **technical alignment**. Perfect match‚Äî**Python**, **AWS** (**Lambda**, **SageMaker**, **DynamoDB**), **AI tools**, **full-stack**, **IaC**. Built exactly these systems at Amazon.

**Third**, **collaboration**. Working with **tech artists**, **data scientists**, **content creators**, **game devs** to deploy **ML models** and build **automation pipelines**. Aligns with my **cross-functional** experience and **AI passion**."

### 3. "Why are you leaving Amazon?" / "What have you been doing since March?"
**Answer**:
"My **team** was **laid off** in **March 2025**‚Äî**organizational restructuring**. Manager, manager's manager‚Äîall laid off. **Beauty Tech team** was being **merged**.

After **5+ years**, I took it as an opportunity to **step back**. **Work on myself**, spend time with **family**. Good break.

Used that time **productively**‚Äîdeepened **ML/AI expertise**. Enrolled in **ML program** covering **EDA**, **Feature Engineering**, **Neural Networks**, **NLP**, **Agentic Frameworks**.

Built **full-stack AI apps**‚Äî**voice assistants**, **real-time transcription**, **health misinformation prevention**. Leveraging **AWS**, **Python**, **AI tools**.

Now **energized** and ready. Want to build **ML cloud apps** that enhance experiences for **millions of fans**."

### 4. "What's your biggest accomplishment?"
**Answer**:
"At Amazon, I built **AI agents** powered by **internal documentation** that answered **CI/CD admin questions** instantly. 

This improved **resolution time** by **82%** and projected savings of **240+ dev-hours** per month.

What made it special was the **end-to-end ownership**. I **identified the problem**, **architected the solution** using **AWS Lambda** and **SageMaker**, built the **RAG pipeline**, and drove **adoption** across the org.

It demonstrated my ability to combine **ML/AI** with **cloud infrastructure** to solve **real business problems**‚Äîexactly what this EA role requires."

### 5. "What's your experience with AWS services mentioned in the JD?"
**Answer**:
"**Extensive hands-on experience**:

**Lambda & API Gateway**: Built **serverless APIs** and **data pipelines**

**SageMaker**: Deployed **ML models** (**Endpoints**, **Batch Transform**)

**DynamoDB**: **Session persistence**, **high-throughput** data storage

**CloudWatch & X-Ray**: Built **4-stage CI/CD pipelines** with **granular monitoring**

**AWS CDK/CloudFormation**: **Infrastructure-as-code** expert, architected entire **deployment pipelines**

**Cognito**: Integrated **authentication systems**

**SAM & SSM**: Used for **serverless app deployment** and **parameter management**

**Step Functions**: Orchestrated complex workflows for **40TB/day** data processing"

### 6. "What's your experience with AI tools like MCP, n8n, coding agents?"
**Answer**:
"I'm a **power user** of modern **AI development tools**:

**Coding agents**: Daily user of **Cursor** and **Windsurf** for **AI-assisted development**

**MCP** (Model Context Protocol): Familiar with the **architecture** and **use cases**

**n8n**: Experience with **workflow automation**

**Generative AI platforms**: **OpenAI**, **Anthropic**, **Gemini**, **Ollama**

**Real-world application**: Built **'Bob'**, my personal **AI voice assistant** with **8 operational modes**. Reduced platform costs by **40x** through **prompt engineering**.

These tools are central to my workflow. I'm excited to leverage them to **accelerate EA's product development cycles**."

### 7. "How do you handle working with cross-functional teams?"
**Answer**:
"At Amazon, I led teams of **8 engineers**, **designers**, and **data scientists**. 

**Key practices**:

**Clear communication**: Led **org-wide documentation workshops**, ensuring everyone had access to **technical reference materials**

**Stakeholder management**: Collaborated with **product managers**, **data scientists**, and **external teams**

**Empowerment**: Enabled **team autonomy** while maintaining **alignment** on goals

**Documentation**: Created **comprehensive technical documentation** for every project

This aligns perfectly with the EA role's need to work with **tech artists**, **content creators**, **data scientists**, and **game engine programmers**."

### 8. "What are your salary expectations?"
**Answer**:
"I'm looking for a **competitive package** that reflects my **5+ years** of experience building **cloud-native ML applications** at Amazon. 

I'm open to discussing the **full compensation package** including **base**, **equity**, and **benefits**. 

What range does EA typically offer for this role?"

### 9. "What's your availability?"
**Answer**:
"I'm **available immediately** and flexible with the **hybrid arrangement** (**3 days/week in office**). 

I'm based in **Vancouver, BC**."

### 10. "Do you have any questions for me?"
**See Questions to Ask section below**

- **OpenAI, Anthropic, Gemini**: API integration experience

---

## ‚ùì Questions to Ask Tyler (HR Recruiter)

### About the Role
1. "What does a typical day look like for this position?"
2. "Who would I be collaborating with most closely? (tech artists, data scientists, game developers?)"
3. ‚≠ê **"What ML/AI projects is the team currently working on or planning?"** (KEY QUESTION)
4. "What AWS services does the team use most heavily?"

### About the Team
5. ‚≠ê **"Can you tell me more about the Marketing Content Production Craft team?"** (KEY QUESTION)
6. "How large is the Fan Growth organization?"
7. "What's the team culture like?"

### About Next Steps
8. "What does the interview process look like after this screen?"
9. "When are you looking to have someone start?"
10. "What's the timeline for next steps?"

### About EA
11. "What makes EA's Fan Growth organization unique compared to other parts of EA?"
12. "How does EA support professional development and learning?"

---

## üö® Red Flags to Avoid

‚ùå **Don't say**:
- Negative things about Amazon or previous employers
- "I don't have experience with X" (reframe as "I haven't used X specifically, but I've used similar tools like Y")
- Appear desperate or over-eager
- Discuss compensation too early (let them bring it up)

‚úÖ **Do say**:
- Specific examples with metrics (82% improvement, 240 dev-hours saved, 40TB/day)
- "That's a great question" (buy yourself thinking time)
- Ask clarifying questions if needed
- Express genuine excitement about EA's mission

---

## üìû Call Logistics Prep

- **Test your setup**: Camera, microphone, internet connection
- **Quiet environment**: No interruptions
- **Have ready**: Resume, JD, this prep guide, notepad
- **Professional background**: Clean, well-lit space
- **Dress code**: Business casual (collared shirt minimum)
- **Join 2-3 minutes early**: Never be late

---

## üéØ Closing Statement

"Thank you for taking the time to speak with me today, **Tyler**. I'm really **excited** about this opportunity. 

The role aligns **perfectly** with my experience building **cloud-native ML applications** at Amazon. I'm particularly drawn to **EA's mission** of creating **engaging experiences** for **millions of fans**. 

I'm confident I can **hit the ground running** with **AWS**, **Python**, and **AI tools** to help accelerate the **Fan Growth team's product development cycles**. 

I look forward to the **next steps**!"

---

- ‚úÖ 5+ years experience (exceeds 4+ requirement)
- ‚úÖ Python + ML expertise

- ‚úÖ Full-stack development
- ‚úÖ IaC (AWS CDK/CloudFormation)
- ‚úÖ Technical documentation
- ‚úÖ Cross-functional team leadership
- ‚úÖ Hybrid work arrangement compatible

# HR Screen Prep Guide - Electronic Arts
## Full Stack Software Engineer - ML Cloud Applications

**Interviewer**: Tyler Poe (HR Recruiter)  
**Company**: Electronic Arts  
**Role**: Full Stack Software Engineer - ML Cloud Applications  
**Team**: Marketing Content Production Craft Team (Fan Growth Organization)

---

## üí° Employment Gap Strategy

**Approach**: Be transparent and authentic
- ‚úÖ **Mention layoff**: "My team and I were laid off in March 2025" (ownership, not personal failure)
- ‚úÖ **Family time**: Spent quality time with family, present for important milestones
- ‚úÖ **Productive learning**: Enrolled in ML program, built full-stack AI applications
- ‚úÖ **Ready & energized**: Expanded skillset, ready to contribute

**Key message**: Turned a challenging situation into an opportunity for growth and family

---

## üéØ Quick Reference - Key Match Points

| **Requirement** | **Your Experience** |
|-----------------|---------------------|
| 4+ years cloud development | ‚úÖ 5+ years at Amazon building AWS cloud-native apps |
| Python + ML proficiency | ‚úÖ Built AI agents, RAG systems, NLP chatbots, ML pipelines |
| AWS services (Lambda, SageMaker, DynamoDB, API Gateway) | ‚úÖ Extensive: Led teams using Lambda, SageMaker, DynamoDB, API Gateway, Step Functions, CDK, CloudWatch |
| AI tools (coding agents, MCP, n8n) | ‚úÖ Heavy user of Cursor, Windsurf, MCP, n8n |
| Full-stack development | ‚úÖ React, TypeScript, Flask, FastAPI, Node.js |
| IaC (CloudFormation) | ‚úÖ AWS CDK & CloudFormation expert, built 4-stage CI/CD pipelines |
| Technical documentation | ‚úÖ Led org-wide documentation workshop at Amazon |
| Cross-functional collaboration | ‚úÖ Led teams of 8 engineers, designers, data scientists |

---

## üìã Common HR Screen Questions & Answers

### 1. "Tell me about yourself"
**Answer (60-90 seconds)**:
"I'm **Aviral Garg**. **5+ years** at **Amazon** building **cloud-native ML applications**. 

Specialize in **full-stack AI solutions** using **AWS**‚Äî**Lambda**, **SageMaker**, **DynamoDB**, **API Gateway**.

At Amazon: Led **8 engineers** building **serverless pipelines** processing **40TB/day**, serving **40M+ customers** monthly. 

Built **AI agents** that improved resolution time by **82%**, saved **240+ dev-hours/month**, reached **100% documentation completion**.

Recent focus: **AI development**‚Äî**voice assistants**, **real-time transcription**, **full-stack AI apps**.

Excited about EA because it combines **AI/ML**, **cloud architecture**, and creating experiences for **millions of fans**."

### 2. "Why are you interested in Electronic Arts?"
**Answer**:
"**Three reasons**:

**First**, **impact at scale**. EA's games reach **hundreds of millions** globally. Grew up hearing "**EA Sports, it's in the game**". Building **ML cloud apps** that enhance these experiences is exciting.

**Second**, **technical alignment**. Perfect match‚Äî**Python**, **AWS** (**Lambda**, **SageMaker**, **DynamoDB**), **AI tools**, **full-stack**, **IaC**. Built exactly these systems at Amazon.

**Third**, **collaboration**. Working with **tech artists**, **data scientists**, **content creators**, **game devs** to deploy **ML models** and build **automation pipelines**. Aligns with my **cross-functional** experience and **AI passion**."

### 3. "Why are you leaving Amazon?" / "What have you been doing since March?"
**Answer**:
"My **team** was **laid off** in **March 2025**‚Äî**organizational restructuring**. Manager, manager's manager‚Äîall laid off. **Beauty Tech team** was being **merged**.

After **5+ years**, I took it as an opportunity to **step back**. **Work on myself**, spend time with **family**. Good break.

Used that time **productively**‚Äîdeepened **ML/AI expertise**. Enrolled in **ML program** covering **EDA**, **Feature Engineering**, **Neural Networks**, **NLP**, **Agentic Frameworks**.

Built **full-stack AI apps**‚Äî**voice assistants**, **real-time transcription**, **health misinformation prevention**. Leveraging **AWS**, **Python**, **AI tools**.

Now **energized** and ready. Want to build **ML cloud apps** that enhance experiences for **millions of fans**."

### 4. "What's your biggest accomplishment?"
**Answer**:
"At Amazon, built **AI agents** powered by **internal docs**‚Äîanswered **CI/CD questions** instantly. 

Improved **resolution time** by **82%**, saved **240+ dev-hours/month**.

**End-to-end ownership**: **Identified problem**, **architected solution** (**Lambda**, **SageMaker**), built **RAG pipeline**, drove **adoption** org-wide.

Demonstrated combining **ML/AI** with **cloud infrastructure** to solve **real business problems**‚Äîexactly what EA needs."

### 5. "What's your experience with AWS services mentioned in the JD?"
**Answer**:
"**Extensive hands-on experience**:

**Lambda & API Gateway**: Built **serverless APIs** and **data pipelines**

**SageMaker**: Deployed **ML models** (**Endpoints**, **Batch Transform**)

**DynamoDB**: **Session persistence**, **high-throughput** data storage

**CloudWatch & X-Ray**: Built **4-stage CI/CD pipelines** with **granular monitoring**

**AWS CDK/CloudFormation**: **Infrastructure-as-code** expert, architected entire **deployment pipelines**

**Cognito**: Integrated **authentication systems**

**SAM & SSM**: Used for **serverless app deployment** and **parameter management**

**Step Functions**: Orchestrated complex workflows for **40TB/day** data processing"

### 6. "What's your experience with AI tools like MCP, n8n, coding agents?"
**Answer**:
"**Power user** of modern **AI dev tools**:

**Coding agents**: Daily user of **Cursor** and **Windsurf** for **AI-assisted development**

**MCP** (Model Context Protocol): Familiar with **architecture** and **use cases**

**n8n**: **Open-source workflow automation** tool for building **low-code automation pipelines**. Experience connecting **APIs**, **databases**, and **AI services** to create **intelligent workflows**. Similar to Zapier but **self-hosted** and **highly customizable**.

**Generative AI**: **OpenAI**, **Anthropic**, **Gemini**, **Ollama**

**Real-world**: Built **'Bob'**‚Äîpersonal **AI voice assistant**, **8 operational modes**. Reduced platform costs **40x** via **prompt engineering**.

These tools are central to my workflow. Excited to leverage them to **accelerate EA's development cycles**."

### 7. "How do you handle working with cross-functional teams?"
**Answer**:
"At Amazon, I led teams of **8 engineers**, **designers**, and **data scientists**. 

**Key practices**:

**Clear communication**: Led **org-wide documentation workshops**, ensuring everyone had access to **technical reference materials**

**Stakeholder management**: Collaborated with **product managers**, **data scientists**, and **external teams**

**Empowerment**: Enabled **team autonomy** while maintaining **alignment** on goals

**Documentation**: Created **comprehensive technical documentation** for every project

This aligns perfectly with the EA role's need to work with **tech artists**, **content creators**, **data scientists**, and **game engine programmers**."

### 8. "What are your salary expectations?"
**Answer**:
"I'm looking for a **competitive package** that reflects my **5+ years** of experience building **cloud-native ML applications** at Amazon. 

I'm open to discussing the **full compensation package** including **base**, **equity**, and **benefits**. 

What range does EA typically offer for this role?"

### 9. "What's your availability?"
**Answer**:
"I'm **available immediately** and flexible with the **hybrid arrangement** (**3 days/week in office**). 

I'm based in **Vancouver, BC**."

### 10. "Do you have any questions for me?"
**See Questions to Ask section below**

---

## üí° Key Talking Points - Memorize These

### Your AWS Expertise (Match to JD)
- **Lambda**: Serverless API development, event-driven architectures
- **SageMaker**: Model deployment (Endpoints, Batch Transform)
- **DynamoDB**: High-throughput NoSQL database for session persistence
- **API Gateway**: RESTful API development and management
- **CloudWatch & X-Ray**: Monitoring, logging, distributed tracing

- Vector databases, RAG, LLMs, model deployment

- **Backend**: Python (Flask, FastAPI), Node.js
- **Databases**: DynamoDB, PostgreSQL, SQLite
- **APIs**: RESTful API design and implementation
- **CI/CD**: GitHub Actions, AWS CDK pipelines
- **IaC**: AWS CDK, CloudFormation

### Your Documentation & Collaboration (Match to JD)

- "Robust documentation & operational readiness" recognition
- Led teams of 8 engineers, designers, data scientists
- Cross-functional collaboration with multiple teams

### Your AI Development Tools (Match to JD)
- **Coding agents**: Cursor, Windsurf (daily use)
- **MCP**: Model Context Protocol familiarity

- **OpenAI, Anthropic, Gemini**: API integration experience

# HR Screen Prep Guide - Electronic Arts
## Full Stack Software Engineer - ML Cloud Applications

**Interviewer**: Tyler Poe (HR Recruiter)  
**Company**: Electronic Arts  
**Role**: Full Stack Software Engineer - ML Cloud Applications  
**Team**: Marketing Content Production Craft Team (Fan Growth Organization)

---

## üí° Employment Gap Strategy

**Approach**: Be transparent and authentic
- ‚úÖ **Mention layoff**: "My team and I were laid off in March 2025" (ownership, not personal failure)
- ‚úÖ **Family time**: Spent quality time with family, present for important milestones
- ‚úÖ **Productive learning**: Enrolled in ML program, built full-stack AI applications
- ‚úÖ **Ready & energized**: Expanded skillset, ready to contribute

**Key message**: Turned a challenging situation into an opportunity for growth and family

---

## üéØ Quick Reference - Key Match Points

| **Requirement** | **Your Experience** |
|-----------------|---------------------|
| 4+ years cloud development | ‚úÖ 5+ years at Amazon building AWS cloud-native apps |
| Python + ML proficiency | ‚úÖ Built AI agents, RAG systems, NLP chatbots, ML pipelines |
| AWS services (Lambda, SageMaker, DynamoDB, API Gateway) | ‚úÖ Extensive: Led teams using Lambda, SageMaker, DynamoDB, API Gateway, Step Functions, CDK, CloudWatch |
| AI tools (coding agents, MCP, n8n) | ‚úÖ Heavy user of Cursor, Windsurf, MCP, n8n |
| Full-stack development | ‚úÖ React, TypeScript, Flask, FastAPI, Node.js |
| IaC (CloudFormation) | ‚úÖ AWS CDK & CloudFormation expert, built 4-stage CI/CD pipelines |
| Technical documentation | ‚úÖ Led org-wide documentation workshop at Amazon |
| Cross-functional collaboration | ‚úÖ Led teams of 8 engineers, designers, data scientists |

---

## üìã Common HR Screen Questions & Answers

### 1. "Tell me about yourself"
**Answer (60-90 seconds)**:
"I'm **Aviral Garg**. **5+ years** at **Amazon** building **cloud-native ML applications**. 

Specialize in **full-stack AI solutions** using **AWS**‚Äî**Lambda**, **SageMaker**, **DynamoDB**, **API Gateway**.

At Amazon: Led **8 engineers** building **serverless pipelines** processing **40TB/day**, serving **40M+ customers** monthly. 

Built **AI agents** that improved resolution time by **82%**, saved **240+ dev-hours/month**, reached **100% documentation completion**.

Recent focus: **AI development**‚Äî**voice assistants**, **real-time transcription**, **full-stack AI apps**.

Excited about EA because it combines **AI/ML**, **cloud architecture**, and creating experiences for **millions of fans**."

### 2. "Why are you interested in Electronic Arts?"
**Answer**:
"**Three reasons**:

**First**, **impact at scale**. EA's games reach **hundreds of millions** globally. Grew up hearing "**EA Sports, it's in the game**". Building **ML cloud apps** that enhance these experiences is exciting.

**Second**, **technical alignment**. Perfect match‚Äî**Python**, **AWS** (**Lambda**, **SageMaker**, **DynamoDB**), **AI tools**, **full-stack**, **IaC**. Built exactly these systems at Amazon.

**Third**, **collaboration**. Working with **tech artists**, **data scientists**, **content creators**, **game devs** to deploy **ML models** and build **automation pipelines**. Aligns with my **cross-functional** experience and **AI passion**."

### 3. "Why are you leaving Amazon?" / "What have you been doing since March?"
**Answer**:
"My **team** was **laid off** in **March 2025**‚Äî**organizational restructuring**. Manager, manager's manager‚Äîall laid off. **Beauty Tech team** was being **merged**.

After **5+ years**, I took it as an opportunity to **step back**. **Work on myself**, spend time with **family**. Good break.

Used that time **productively**‚Äîdeepened **ML/AI expertise**. Enrolled in **ML program** covering **EDA**, **Feature Engineering**, **Neural Networks**, **NLP**, **Agentic Frameworks**.

Built **full-stack AI apps**‚Äî**voice assistants**, **real-time transcription**, **health misinformation prevention**. Leveraging **AWS**, **Python**, **AI tools**.

Now **energized** and ready. Want to build **ML cloud apps** that enhance experiences for **millions of fans**."

### 4. "What's your biggest accomplishment?"
**Answer**:
"At Amazon, built **AI agents** powered by **internal docs**‚Äîanswered **CI/CD questions** instantly. 

Improved **resolution time** by **82%**, saved **240+ dev-hours/month**.

**End-to-end ownership**: **Identified problem**, **architected solution** (**Lambda**, **SageMaker**), built **RAG pipeline**, drove **adoption** org-wide.

Demonstrated combining **ML/AI** with **cloud infrastructure** to solve **real business problems**‚Äîexactly what EA needs."

### 5. "What's your experience with AWS services mentioned in the JD?"
**Answer**:
"**Extensive hands-on experience**:

**Lambda & API Gateway**: Built **serverless APIs** and **data pipelines**

**SageMaker**: Deployed **ML models** (**Endpoints**, **Batch Transform**)

**DynamoDB**: **Session persistence**, **high-throughput** data storage

**CloudWatch & X-Ray**: Built **4-stage CI/CD pipelines** with **granular monitoring**

**AWS CDK/CloudFormation**: **Infrastructure-as-code** expert, architected entire **deployment pipelines**

**Cognito**: Integrated **authentication systems**

**SAM & SSM**: Used for **serverless app deployment** and **parameter management**

**Step Functions**: Orchestrated complex workflows for **40TB/day** data processing"

### 6. "What's your experience with AI tools like MCP, n8n, coding agents?"
**Answer**:
"**Power user** of modern **AI dev tools**:

**Coding agents**: Daily user of **Cursor** and **Windsurf** for **AI-assisted development**

**MCP** (Model Context Protocol): Familiar with **architecture** and **use cases**

**n8n**: **Open-source workflow automation** tool for building **low-code automation pipelines**. Experience connecting **APIs**, **databases**, and **AI services** to create **intelligent workflows**. Similar to Zapier but **self-hosted** and **highly customizable**.

**Generative AI**: **OpenAI**, **Anthropic**, **Gemini**, **Ollama**

**Real-world**: Built **'Bob'**‚Äîpersonal **AI voice assistant**, **8 operational modes**. Reduced platform costs **40x** via **prompt engineering**.

These tools are central to my workflow. Excited to leverage them to **accelerate EA's development cycles**."

### 7. "How do you handle working with cross-functional teams?"
**Answer**:
"At Amazon, led teams of **8 engineers**, **designers**, **data scientists**. 

**Key practices**:

**Clear communication**: Led **org-wide documentation workshops**‚Äîeveryone had access to **technical references**

**Stakeholder management**: Collaborated with **PMs**, **data scientists**, **external teams**

**Empowerment**: **Team autonomy** while maintaining **alignment**

**Documentation**: **Comprehensive technical docs** for every project

Aligns with EA's need for **tech artists**, **content creators**, **data scientists**, **game engine programmers**."

### 8. "What are your salary expectations?"
**Answer**:
"Looking for **competitive package** reflecting **5+ years** building **cloud-native ML apps** at Amazon. 

Open to discussing **full comp**‚Äî**base**, **equity**, **benefits**. 

What range does EA typically offer?"

### 9. "What's your availability?"
**Answer**:
"**Available immediately**. Flexible with **hybrid** (**3 days/week in office**). Based in **Vancouver, BC**."

### 10. "Do you have any questions for me?"
**See Questions to Ask section below**

---

## üí° Key Talking Points - Memorize These

### Your AWS Expertise (Match to JD)
- **Lambda**: Serverless API development, event-driven architectures
- **SageMaker**: Model deployment (Endpoints, Batch Transform)
- **DynamoDB**: High-throughput NoSQL database for session persistence
- **API Gateway**: RESTful API development and management
- **CloudWatch & X-Ray**: Monitoring, logging, distributed tracing
- **AWS CDK/CloudFormation**: Infrastructure-as-code, CI/CD pipelines
- **Cognito**: Authentication and authorization
- **SAM & SSM**: Serverless Application Model, Systems Manager
- **Step Functions**: Workflow orchestration

### Your AI/ML Experience (Match to JD)
- Built AI agents for documentation Q&A (RAG pipeline)
- Deployed NLP chatbots with full CI/CD
- Integrated OpenAI Whisper for local ML-based speech recognition
- Health misinformation prevention system with multi-agent simulation
- Experience with OpenAI, Anthropic, Gemini, Ollama
- Vector databases, RAG, LLMs, model deployment

### Your Full-Stack Expertise (Match to JD)
- **Frontend**: React 19, TypeScript
- **Backend**: Python (Flask, FastAPI), Node.js
- **Databases**: DynamoDB, PostgreSQL, SQLite
- **APIs**: RESTful API design and implementation
- **CI/CD**: GitHub Actions, AWS CDK pipelines
- **IaC**: AWS CDK, CloudFormation

### Your Documentation & Collaboration (Match to JD)
- Led org-wide documentation workshop at Amazon
- "Robust documentation & operational readiness" recognition
- Led teams of 8 engineers, designers, data scientists
- Cross-functional collaboration with multiple teams

### Your AI Development Tools (Match to JD)
- **Coding agents**: Cursor, Windsurf (daily use)
- **MCP**: Model Context Protocol familiarity
- **n8n**: Workflow automation
- **OpenAI, Anthropic, Gemini**: API integration experience

- Express genuine excitement about EA's mission

# Aviral Garg
Vancouver, British Columbia, Canada ¬∑ aviral.garg@icloud.com ¬∑ in/aviralgarg ¬∑ aviralgarg.com

---

## SKILLS

- **AI & Machine Learning:** **Generative AI** (**OpenAI**, **Anthropic**, **Gemini**, **Ollama**), **Agentic Orchestration & Frameworks**, **MCP**, **RAG**, **NLP**, **LLMs**, **Model Deployment** (**SageMaker Endpoints**, **Batch Transform**), Vector Databases, **Python (ML Libraries)**
- **Cloud & DevOps (AWS):** **Lambda**, **SageMaker**, **API Gateway**, **DynamoDB**, **Cognito**, **AWS CDK & CloudFormation (IaC)**, **SAM**, **SSM**, **Step Functions**, S3, EC2, ECS, **CloudWatch**, **X-Ray**, SNS, SQS, Glue, Athena 
- **Languages & Frameworks:** **Python** (**Flask**, **FastAPI**), **Node.js**, **React**, **TypeScript**, Kotlin, C#
- **Developer Tools & Version Control:** **Git**, Docker, **Cursor**, **Windsurf**, Linear, Playwright, Unity3D, **n8n**

---

## EXPERIENCE

### Software Development Engineer ‚Äî Amazon ¬∑ Beauty Tech Team
*February 2021 ‚Äì March 2025 ¬∑ Vancouver, BC*

- Led a team of 8 engineers, designers, & data scientists to deploy serverless data pipelines with 50% increased efficiency.
- Leveraged AWS Step Functions, Lambda, DynamoDB, SageMaker, & Athena; automatically scaled for growth, processed 40TB/day of product catalog data, & served 40M+ monthly customers across 15+ countries.
- Built 4-staged AWS CDK CI/CD pipelines using CloudWatch & X-Ray for granular system monitoring & bottleneck tracing. Received org-wide accolades for robust documentation & operational readiness for every step of the SDLC.
- Built internal-documentation-powered AI agents to provide instant answers to CI/CD admin questions, identify documentation gaps, & flag outdated content. Improved question resolution time by 82%, with projected savings of 240+ dev-hrs/month from integration with the internal admin ticketing system.
- Led an organization-wide documentation workshop, establishing a systematic platform for subject-matter-expert reference & reaching 100% completion of product & CI/CD documentation for the Beauty Tech organization.
- Spearheaded CI/CD-driven store-page-builder project for Amazon clients using React & Python.
- Integrated external microservices & A/B testing framework, increasing client customization capabilities by 300%.
- Automated monthly business reports for the recommendations team, reducing manual reporting time by 90%.
- Led a team of 4 to win first place at the Amazon 2022 Hackathon with an Augmented Reality iOS makeup-tutorial app.

### Software Development Engineer ‚Äî Amazon ¬∑ Prime Pantry Team
*June 2020 ‚Äì February 2021 ¬∑ Vancouver, BC*

- Architected robust Kotlin applications achieving 100% test coverage for Prime Pantry API development.
- Optimized API performance, reducing page-load impact by 37% & increasing add-to-cart conversion rates by 2.5%, which directly contributed to over $3 million monthly revenue for the Prime Pantry platform.
- Cut setup time by 75% & saved 3,528 dev-hrs/year by automating Prime Pantry API developer onboarding & environment setup while eliminating setup-related errors.
- Built automated CI/CD pipelines in AWS CDK, saving 12+ dev-hrs/week & cutting deployment errors by 95%.
- Delivered $30K in annual cost savings through systematic AWS CI/CD optimization & usage policy implementation.

### Pre-bunker health communications system - Health Misinformation Prevention
[github.com/gaviral/pre_bunker_health_communications_system](https://github.com/gaviral/pre_bunker_health_communications_system)

- Built AI agents for health misinformation prevention, simulating public reactions & generating evidence-backed prebunks.
- Created a comprehensive prototype with implementation across 19 versions achieving 65-80% risk reduction.
- Built a 5-stage pipeline: Claim Extraction, Risk Assessment, Audience Simulation, Evidence Validation, Countermeasures.
- Developed 12 specialized agent personas for comprehensive audience simulation with multi-source evidence validation.
- Created a FastAPI web interface with async processing & real-time risk assessment.
- Developed a novel Misinterpretability@k metric for quantifying health communication risk.

- Built full-stack GPT-powered AI app with LangChain on AWS Lambda, API Gateway, DynamoDB, S3 & CloudFront.
- Created a React 19 + TypeScript frontend with a CI/CD pipeline using GitHub Actions, deploying to production.
- Implemented session persistence with DynamoDB TTL & contextual follow-up chat system.

### Stock Gainers - Real-Time Market Tracker
- Built a real-time stock market tracking application with FastAPI & SQLAlchemy ORM supporting PostgreSQL & SQLite.
- Integrated the Yahoo Finance API for real-time data with a comprehensive user authentication system using AWS Cognito.
- Created an admin dashboard for database management with a responsive Bootstrap UI & color-coded visualization.
- Deployed the application to production on AWS with auto-refresh mechanism & custom stock symbol tracking.

# HR Screen Prep Guide - Electronic Arts
## Full Stack Software Engineer - ML Cloud Applications

**Interviewer**: Tyler Poe (HR Recruiter)  
**Company**: Electronic Arts  
**Role**: Full Stack Software Engineer - ML Cloud Applications  
**Team**: Marketing Content Production Craft Team (Fan Growth Organization)

---

## üí° Employment Gap Strategy

**Approach**: Be transparent and authentic
- ‚úÖ **Mention layoff**: "My team and I were laid off in March 2025" (ownership, not personal failure)
- ‚úÖ **Family time**: Spent quality time with family, present for important milestones
- ‚úÖ **Productive learning**: Enrolled in ML program, built full-stack AI applications
- ‚úÖ **Ready & energized**: Expanded skillset, ready to contribute

**Key message**: Turned a challenging situation into an opportunity for growth and family

---

## üéØ Quick Reference - Key Match Points

| **Requirement** | **Your Experience** |
|-----------------|---------------------|
| 4+ years cloud development | ‚úÖ 5+ years at Amazon building AWS cloud-native apps |
| Python + ML proficiency | ‚úÖ Built AI agents, RAG systems, NLP chatbots, ML pipelines |
| AWS services (Lambda, SageMaker, DynamoDB, API Gateway) | ‚úÖ Extensive: Led teams using Lambda, SageMaker, DynamoDB, API Gateway, Step Functions, CDK, CloudWatch |
| AI tools (coding agents, MCP, n8n) | ‚úÖ Heavy user of Cursor, Windsurf, MCP, n8n |
| Full-stack development | ‚úÖ React, TypeScript, Flask, FastAPI, Node.js |
| IaC (CloudFormation) | ‚úÖ AWS CDK & CloudFormation expert, built 4-stage CI/CD pipelines |
| Technical documentation | ‚úÖ Led org-wide documentation workshop at Amazon |
| Cross-functional collaboration | ‚úÖ Led teams of 8 engineers, designers, data scientists |

## üìã Common HR Screen Questions & Answers

### 1. "Tell me about yourself"
**Answer (60-90 seconds)**:
- **Aviral Garg**. 5+ years at Amazon building **cloud-native ML apps**
  - Specialize in **full-stack AI solutions**
  - Using **AWS**: Lambda, SageMaker, DynamoDB, API Gateway

- At Amazon:
  - Led 8 engineers building **serverless pipelines**
    - Processing 40TB/day
    - Serving 40M+ customers monthly
  - Built **AI agents** for internal docs
    - Improved resolution time 82%
    - Saved 240+ dev-hours/month
    - Reached 100% documentation completion

- Recent focus: **AI development**
  - Voice assistants, real-time transcription, full-stack AI apps

- Excited about EA:
  - Combines **AI/ML**, **cloud**, creating experiences for millions of fans

### 2. "Why are you interested in Electronic Arts?"
**Answer**:
"**Three reasons**:

**First**, **impact at scale**. EA's games reach **hundreds of millions** globally. Grew up hearing "**EA Sports, it's in the game**". Building **ML cloud apps** that enhance these experiences is exciting.

**Second**, **technical alignment**. Perfect match‚Äî**Python**, **AWS** (**Lambda**, **SageMaker**, **DynamoDB**), **AI tools**, **full-stack**, **IaC**. Built exactly these systems at Amazon.

**Third**, **collaboration**. Working with **tech artists**, **data scientists**, **content creators**, **game devs** to deploy **ML models** and build **automation pipelines**. Aligns with my **cross-functional** experience and **AI passion**."

### 3. "Why are you leaving Amazon?" / "What have you been doing since March?"
**Answer**:
"My **team** was **laid off** in **March 2025**‚Äî**organizational restructuring**. Manager, manager's manager‚Äîall laid off. **Beauty Tech team** was being **merged**.

After **5+ years**, I took it as an opportunity to **step back**. **Work on myself**, spend time with **family**. Good break.

Used that time **productively**‚Äîdeepened **ML/AI expertise**. Enrolled in **ML program** covering **EDA**, **Feature Engineering**, **Neural Networks**, **NLP**, **Agentic Frameworks**.

Built **full-stack AI apps**‚Äî**voice assistants**, **real-time transcription**, **health misinformation prevention**. Leveraging **AWS**, **Python**, **AI tools**.

Now **energized** and ready. Want to build **ML cloud apps** that enhance experiences for **millions of fans**."

### 4. "What's your biggest accomplishment?"
**Answer**:
"At Amazon, built **AI agents** powered by **internal docs**‚Äîanswered **CI/CD questions** instantly. 

Improved **resolution time** by **82%**, saved **240+ dev-hours/month**.

**End-to-end ownership**: **Identified problem**, **architected solution** (**Lambda**, **SageMaker**), built **RAG pipeline**, drove **adoption** org-wide.

Demonstrated combining **ML/AI** with **cloud infrastructure** to solve **real business problems**‚Äîexactly what EA needs."

### 5. "What's your experience with AWS services mentioned in the JD?"
**Answer**:
"**Extensive hands-on experience**:

**Lambda & API Gateway**: Built **serverless APIs** and **data pipelines**

**SageMaker**: Deployed **ML models** (**Endpoints**, **Batch Transform**)

**DynamoDB**: **Session persistence**, **high-throughput** data storage

**CloudWatch & X-Ray**: Built **4-stage CI/CD pipelines** with **granular monitoring**

**AWS CDK/CloudFormation**: **Infrastructure-as-code** expert, architected entire **deployment pipelines**

**Cognito**: Integrated **authentication systems**

**SAM & SSM**: Used for **serverless app deployment** and **parameter management**

**Step Functions**: Orchestrated complex workflows for **40TB/day** data processing"

### 6. "What's your experience with AI tools like MCP, n8n, coding agents?"
**Answer**:
"**Power user** of modern **AI dev tools**:

**Coding agents**: Daily user of **Cursor** and **Windsurf** for **AI-assisted development**

**MCP** (Model Context Protocol): Familiar with **architecture** and **use cases**

**n8n**: **Open-source workflow automation** tool for building **low-code automation pipelines**. Experience connecting **APIs**, **databases**, and **AI services** to create **intelligent workflows**. Similar to Zapier but **self-hosted** and **highly customizable**.

**Generative AI**: **OpenAI**, **Anthropic**, **Gemini**, **Ollama**

**Real-world**: Built **'Bob'**‚Äîpersonal **AI voice assistant**, **8 operational modes**. Reduced platform costs **40x** via **prompt engineering**.

These tools are central to my workflow. Excited to leverage them to **accelerate EA's development cycles**."

### 7. "How do you handle working with cross-functional teams?"
**Answer**:
"At Amazon, led teams of **8 engineers**, **designers**, **data scientists**. 

**Key practices**:

**Clear communication**: Led **org-wide documentation workshops**‚Äîeveryone had access to **technical references**

**Stakeholder management**: Collaborated with **PMs**, **data scientists**, **external teams**

**Empowerment**: **Team autonomy** while maintaining **alignment**

**Documentation**: **Comprehensive technical docs** for every project

Aligns with EA's need for **tech artists**, **content creators**, **data scientists**, **game engine programmers**."

### 8. "What are your salary expectations?"
**Answer**:
"Looking for **competitive package** reflecting **5+ years** building **cloud-native ML apps** at Amazon. 

Open to discussing **full comp**‚Äî**base**, **equity**, **benefits**. 

What range does EA typically offer?"

### 9. "What's your availability?"
**Answer**:
"**Available immediately**. Flexible with **hybrid** (**3 days/week in office**). Based in **Vancouver, BC**."

### 10. "Do you have any questions for me?"
**See Questions to Ask section below**

---

## üí° Key Talking Points - Memorize These

### Your AWS Expertise (Match to JD)
- **Lambda**: Serverless API development, event-driven architectures
- **SageMaker**: Model deployment (Endpoints, Batch Transform)
- **DynamoDB**: High-throughput NoSQL database for session persistence
- **API Gateway**: RESTful API development and management
- **CloudWatch & X-Ray**: Monitoring, logging, distributed tracing
- **AWS CDK/CloudFormation**: Infrastructure-as-code, CI/CD pipelines
- **Cognito**: Authentication and authorization
- **SAM & SSM**: Serverless Application Model, Systems Manager
- **Step Functions**: Workflow orchestration

### Your AI/ML Experience (Match to JD)
- Built AI agents for documentation Q&A (RAG pipeline)
- Deployed NLP chatbots with full CI/CD
- Integrated OpenAI Whisper for local ML-based speech recognition
- Health misinformation prevention system with multi-agent simulation
- Experience with OpenAI, Anthropic, Gemini, Ollama
- Vector databases, RAG, LLMs, model deployment

### Your Full-Stack Expertise (Match to JD)
- **Frontend**: React 19, TypeScript
- **Backend**: Python (Flask, FastAPI), Node.js
- **Databases**: DynamoDB, PostgreSQL, SQLite
- **APIs**: RESTful API design and implementation
- **CI/CD**: GitHub Actions, AWS CDK pipelines
- **IaC**: AWS CDK, CloudFormation

### Your Documentation & Collaboration (Match to JD)
- Led org-wide documentation workshop at Amazon
- "Robust documentation & operational readiness" recognition
- Led teams of 8 engineers, designers, data scientists
- Cross-functional collaboration with multiple teams

### Your AI Development Tools (Match to JD)
- **Coding agents**: Cursor, Windsurf (daily use)
- **MCP**: Model Context Protocol familiarity
- **n8n**: Workflow automation
- **OpenAI, Anthropic, Gemini**: API integration experience

## üö® Red Flags to Avoid

‚ùå **Don't say**:
- Negative things about Amazon or previous employers
- "I don't have experience with X" (reframe as "I haven't used X specifically, but I've used similar tools like Y")
- Appear desperate or over-eager
- Discuss compensation too early (let them bring it up)

‚úÖ **Do say**:
- Specific examples with metrics (82% improvement, 240 dev-hours saved, 40TB/day)
- "That's a great question" (buy yourself thinking time)
- Ask clarifying questions if needed
- Express genuine excitement about EA's mission

- **Have ready**: Resume, JD, this prep guide, notepad
- **Professional background**: Clean, well-lit space
- **Dress code**: Business casual (collared shirt minimum)
- **Join 2-3 minutes early**: Never be late

Confident I can **hit the ground running** with **AWS**, **Python**, **AI tools** to accelerate **Fan Growth's development cycles**. 

Looking forward to **next steps**!"

# HR Screen Prep Guide - Electronic Arts
## Full Stack Software Engineer - ML Cloud Applications

**Interviewer**: Tyler Poe (HR Recruiter)  
**Company**: Electronic Arts  
**Role**: Full Stack Software Engineer - ML Cloud Applications  
**Team**: Marketing Content Production Craft Team (Fan Growth Organization)

---

## üí° Employment Gap Strategy

**Approach**: Be transparent and authentic
- ‚úÖ **Mention layoff**: "My team and I were laid off in March 2025" (ownership, not personal failure)
- ‚úÖ **Family time**: Spent quality time with family, present for important milestones
- ‚úÖ **Productive learning**: Enrolled in ML program, built full-stack AI applications
- ‚úÖ **Ready & energized**: Expanded skillset, ready to contribute

**Key message**: Turned a challenging situation into an opportunity for growth and family

---

## üéØ Quick Reference - Key Match Points

| **Requirement** | **Your Experience** |
|-----------------|---------------------|
| 4+ years cloud development | ‚úÖ 5+ years at Amazon building AWS cloud-native apps |
| Python + ML proficiency | ‚úÖ Built AI agents, RAG systems, NLP chatbots, ML pipelines |
| AWS services (Lambda, SageMaker, DynamoDB, API Gateway) | ‚úÖ Extensive: Led teams using Lambda, SageMaker, DynamoDB, API Gateway, Step Functions, CDK, CloudWatch |
| AI tools (coding agents, MCP, n8n) | ‚úÖ Heavy user of Cursor, Windsurf, MCP, n8n |
| Full-stack development | ‚úÖ React, TypeScript, Flask, FastAPI, Node.js |
| IaC (CloudFormation) | ‚úÖ AWS CDK & CloudFormation expert, built 4-stage CI/CD pipelines |
| Technical documentation | ‚úÖ Led org-wide documentation workshop at Amazon |
| Cross-functional collaboration | ‚úÖ Led teams of 8 engineers, designers, data scientists |

---

## üìã Common HR Screen Questions & Answers

### 1. "Tell me about yourself"
**Answer (60-90 seconds)**:
- **Aviral Garg**. 5+ years at Amazon building **cloud-native ML apps**
  - Specialize in **full-stack AI solutions**
  - Using **AWS**: Lambda, SageMaker, DynamoDB, API Gateway

- At Amazon:
  - Led 8 engineers building **serverless pipelines**
    - Processing 40TB/day
    - Serving 40M+ customers monthly
  - Built **AI agents** for internal docs
    - Improved resolution time 82%
    - Saved 240+ dev-hours/month
    - Reached 100% documentation completion

- Recent focus: **AI development**
  - Voice assistants, real-time transcription, full-stack AI apps

- Excited about EA:
  - Combines **AI/ML**, **cloud**, creating experiences for millions of fans

### 2. "Why are you interested in Electronic Arts?"
**Answer**:
Three reasons:

- **Impact at scale**
  - EA games reach hundreds of millions globally
  - Grew up hearing "EA Sports, it's in the game"
  - Building ML cloud apps that enhance these experiences

- **Technical alignment**
  - Perfect match: Python, AWS (Lambda, SageMaker, DynamoDB), AI tools, full-stack, IaC
  - Built exactly these systems at Amazon

- **Collaboration**
  - Work with tech artists, data scientists, content creators, game devs
  - Deploy ML models, build automation pipelines
  - Aligns with my cross-functional experience

### 3. "Why are you leaving Amazon?" / "What have you been doing since March?"
**Answer**:
"My **team** was **laid off** in **March 2025**‚Äî**organizational restructuring**. Manager, manager's manager‚Äîall laid off. **Beauty Tech team** was being **merged**.

After **5+ years**, I took it as an opportunity to **step back**. **Work on myself**, spend time with **family**. Good break.

Used that time **productively**‚Äîdeepened **ML/AI expertise**. Enrolled in **ML program** covering **EDA**, **Feature Engineering**, **Neural Networks**, **NLP**, **Agentic Frameworks**.

Built **full-stack AI apps**‚Äî**voice assistants**, **real-time transcription**, **health misinformation prevention**. Leveraging **AWS**, **Python**, **AI tools**.

Now **energized** and ready. Want to build **ML cloud apps** that enhance experiences for **millions of fans**."

### 4. "What's your biggest accomplishment?"
**Answer**:
"At Amazon, built **AI agents** powered by **internal docs**‚Äîanswered **CI/CD questions** instantly. 

Improved **resolution time** by **82%**, saved **240+ dev-hours/month**.

**End-to-end ownership**: **Identified problem**, **architected solution** (**Lambda**, **SageMaker**), built **RAG pipeline**, drove **adoption** org-wide.

Demonstrated combining **ML/AI** with **cloud infrastructure** to solve **real business problems**‚Äîexactly what EA needs."

### 5. "What's your experience with AWS services mentioned in the JD?"
**Answer**:
"**Extensive hands-on experience**:

**Lambda & API Gateway**: Built **serverless APIs** and **data pipelines**

**SageMaker**: Deployed **ML models** (**Endpoints**, **Batch Transform**)

**DynamoDB**: **Session persistence**, **high-throughput** data storage

**CloudWatch & X-Ray**: Built **4-stage CI/CD pipelines** with **granular monitoring**

**AWS CDK/CloudFormation**: **Infrastructure-as-code** expert, architected entire **deployment pipelines**

**Cognito**: Integrated **authentication systems**

**SAM & SSM**: Used for **serverless app deployment** and **parameter management**

**Step Functions**: Orchestrated complex workflows for **40TB/day** data processing"

### 6. "What's your experience with AI tools like MCP, n8n, coding agents?"
**Answer**:
"**Power user** of modern **AI dev tools**:

**Coding agents**: Daily user of **Cursor** and **Windsurf** for **AI-assisted development**

**MCP** (Model Context Protocol): Familiar with **architecture** and **use cases**

**n8n**: **Open-source workflow automation** tool for building **low-code automation pipelines**. Experience connecting **APIs**, **databases**, and **AI services** to create **intelligent workflows**. Similar to Zapier but **self-hosted** and **highly customizable**.

**Generative AI**: **OpenAI**, **Anthropic**, **Gemini**, **Ollama**

**Real-world**: Built **'Bob'**‚Äîpersonal **AI voice assistant**, **8 operational modes**. Reduced platform costs **40x** via **prompt engineering**.

These tools are central to my workflow. Excited to leverage them to **accelerate EA's development cycles**."

### 7. "How do you handle working with cross-functional teams?"
**Answer**:
"At Amazon, led teams of **8 engineers**, **designers**, **data scientists**. 

**Key practices**:

**Clear communication**: Led **org-wide documentation workshops**‚Äîeveryone had access to **technical references**

**Stakeholder management**: Collaborated with **PMs**, **data scientists**, **external teams**

**Empowerment**: **Team autonomy** while maintaining **alignment**

**Documentation**: **Comprehensive technical docs** for every project

Aligns with EA's need for **tech artists**, **content creators**, **data scientists**, **game engine programmers**."

### 8. "What are your salary expectations?"
**Answer**:
"Looking for **competitive package** reflecting **5+ years** building **cloud-native ML apps** at Amazon. 

Open to discussing **full comp**‚Äî**base**, **equity**, **benefits**. 

What range does EA typically offer?"

### 9. "What's your availability?"
**Answer**:
"**Available immediately**. Flexible with **hybrid** (**3 days/week in office**). Based in **Vancouver, BC**."

### 10. "Do you have any questions for me?"
**See Questions to Ask section below**

7. "What's the team culture like?"

### About Next Steps
8. "What does the interview process look like after this screen?"
9. "When are you looking to have someone start?"
10. "What's the timeline for next steps?"

### About EA
11. "What makes EA's Fan Growth organization unique compared to other parts of EA?"
12. "How does EA support professional development and learning?"

---

## üö® Red Flags to Avoid

‚ùå **Don't say**:
- Negative things about Amazon or previous employers
- "I don't have experience with X" (reframe as "I haven't used X specifically, but I've used similar tools like Y")
- Appear desperate or over-eager
- Discuss compensation too early (let them bring it up)

‚úÖ **Do say**:
- Specific examples with metrics (82% improvement, 240 dev-hours saved, 40TB/day)
- "That's a great question" (buy yourself thinking time)
- Ask clarifying questions if needed
- Express genuine excitement about EA's mission

---

## üìû Call Logistics Prep

- **Test your setup**: Camera, microphone, internet connection
- **Quiet environment**: No interruptions
- **Have ready**: Resume, JD, this prep guide, notepad
- **Professional background**: Clean, well-lit space
- **Dress code**: Business casual (collared shirt minimum)
- **Join 2-3 minutes early**: Never be late

---

## üéØ Closing Statement

"Thanks for your time today, **Tyler**. Really **excited** about this opportunity. 

Role aligns **perfectly** with my experience building **cloud-native ML apps** at Amazon. Drawn to **EA's mission** of creating **engaging experiences** for **millions of fans**. 

Confident I can **hit the ground running** with **AWS**, **Python**, **AI tools** to accelerate **Fan Growth's development cycles**. 

Looking forward to **next steps**!"

---

## üìä Your Match Score: 95%

- ‚úÖ 5+ years experience (exceeds 4+ requirement)

- ‚úÖ AWS services (all mentioned services)

# HR Screen Prep Guide - Electronic Arts
## Full Stack Software Engineer - ML Cloud Applications

**Interviewer**: Tyler Poe (HR Recruiter)  
**Company**: Electronic Arts  
**Role**: Full Stack Software Engineer - ML Cloud Applications  
**Team**: Marketing Content Production Craft Team (Fan Growth Organization)

---

## üí° Employment Gap Strategy

**Approach**: Be transparent and authentic
- ‚úÖ **Mention layoff**: "My team and I were laid off in March 2025" (ownership, not personal failure)
- ‚úÖ **Family time**: Spent quality time with family, present for important milestones
- ‚úÖ **Productive learning**: Enrolled in ML program, built full-stack AI applications
- ‚úÖ **Ready & energized**: Expanded skillset, ready to contribute

**Key message**: Turned a challenging situation into an opportunity for growth and family

---

## üéØ Quick Reference - Key Match Points

| **Requirement** | **Your Experience** |
|-----------------|---------------------|
| 4+ years cloud development | ‚úÖ 5+ years at Amazon building AWS cloud-native apps |
| Python + ML proficiency | ‚úÖ Built AI agents, RAG systems, NLP chatbots, ML pipelines |
| AWS services (Lambda, SageMaker, DynamoDB, API Gateway) | ‚úÖ Extensive: Led teams using Lambda, SageMaker, DynamoDB, API Gateway, Step Functions, CDK, CloudWatch |
| AI tools (coding agents, MCP, n8n) | ‚úÖ Heavy user of Cursor, Windsurf, MCP, n8n |
| Full-stack development | ‚úÖ React, TypeScript, Flask, FastAPI, Node.js |
| IaC (CloudFormation) | ‚úÖ AWS CDK & CloudFormation expert, built 4-stage CI/CD pipelines |
| Technical documentation | ‚úÖ Led org-wide documentation workshop at Amazon |
| Cross-functional collaboration | ‚úÖ Led teams of 8 engineers, designers, data scientists |

---

## üìã Common HR Screen Questions & Answers

### 1. "Tell me about yourself"
**Answer (60-90 seconds)**:
- **Aviral Garg**. 5+ years at Amazon building **cloud-native ML apps**
  - Specialize in **full-stack AI solutions**
  - Using **AWS**: Lambda, SageMaker, DynamoDB, API Gateway

- At Amazon:
  - Led 8 engineers building **serverless pipelines**
    - Processing 40TB/day
    - Serving 40M+ customers monthly
  - Built **AI agents** for internal docs
    - Improved resolution time 82%
    - Saved 240+ dev-hours/month
    - Reached 100% documentation completion

- Recent focus: **AI development**
  - Voice assistants, real-time transcription, full-stack AI apps

- Excited about EA:
  - Combines **AI/ML**, **cloud**, creating experiences for millions of fans

### 2. "Why are you interested in Electronic Arts?"
**Answer**:
Three reasons:

- **Impact at scale**
  - EA games reach hundreds of millions globally
  - Grew up hearing "EA Sports, it's in the game"
  - Building ML cloud apps that enhance these experiences

- **Technical alignment**
  - Perfect match: Python, AWS (Lambda, SageMaker, DynamoDB), AI tools, full-stack, IaC
  - Built exactly these systems at Amazon

- **Collaboration**
  - Work with tech artists, data scientists, content creators, game devs
  - Deploy ML models, build automation pipelines
  - Aligns with my cross-functional experience

### 3. "Why are you leaving Amazon?" / "What have you been doing since March?"
**Answer**:
- **Laid off** March 2025
  - Organizational restructuring
  - Manager, manager's manager‚Äîall laid off
  - Beauty Tech team being merged

- After 5+ years, took opportunity to:
  - **Step back**, work on myself
  - Spend time with family
  - Good break

- Used time **productively**:
  - Deepened **ML/AI expertise**
    - Enrolled in ML program: EDA, Feature Engineering, Neural Networks, NLP, Agentic Frameworks
  - Built **full-stack AI apps**:
    - Voice assistants
    - Real-time transcription
    - Health misinformation prevention
    - Using AWS, Python, AI tools

- Now **energized** and ready
  - Want to build ML cloud apps for millions of fans

### 4. "What's your biggest accomplishment?"
**Answer**:
- At Amazon: built **AI agents** powered by internal docs
  - Answered CI/CD questions instantly
  - Improved resolution time 82%
  - Saved 240+ dev-hours/month

- **End-to-end ownership**:
  - Identified problem
  - Architected solution (Lambda, SageMaker)
  - Built RAG pipeline
  - Drove adoption org-wide

- Demonstrated: combining **ML/AI** with **cloud infrastructure**
  - Solve real business problems
  - Exactly what EA needs

### 5. "What's your experience with AWS services mentioned in the JD?"
**Answer**:
"**Extensive hands-on experience**:

**Lambda & API Gateway**: Built **serverless APIs** and **data pipelines**

**SageMaker**: Deployed **ML models** (**Endpoints**, **Batch Transform**)

**DynamoDB**: **Session persistence**, **high-throughput** data storage

**CloudWatch & X-Ray**: Built **4-stage CI/CD pipelines** with **granular monitoring**

**AWS CDK/CloudFormation**: **Infrastructure-as-code** expert, architected entire **deployment pipelines**

**Cognito**: Integrated **authentication systems**

**SAM & SSM**: Used for **serverless app deployment** and **parameter management**

**Step Functions**: Orchestrated complex workflows for **40TB/day** data processing"

### 6. "What's your experience with AI tools like MCP, n8n, coding agents?"
**Answer**:
"**Power user** of modern **AI dev tools**:

**Coding agents**: Daily user of **Cursor** and **Windsurf** for **AI-assisted development**

**MCP** (Model Context Protocol): Familiar with **architecture** and **use cases**

**n8n**: **Open-source workflow automation** tool for building **low-code automation pipelines**. Experience connecting **APIs**, **databases**, and **AI services** to create **intelligent workflows**. Similar to Zapier but **self-hosted** and **highly customizable**.

**Generative AI**: **OpenAI**, **Anthropic**, **Gemini**, **Ollama**

**Real-world**: Built **'Bob'**‚Äîpersonal **AI voice assistant**, **8 operational modes**. Reduced platform costs **40x** via **prompt engineering**.

These tools are central to my workflow. Excited to leverage them to **accelerate EA's development cycles**."

### 7. "How do you handle working with cross-functional teams?"
**Answer**:
"At Amazon, led teams of **8 engineers**, **designers**, **data scientists**. 

**Key practices**:

**Clear communication**: Led **org-wide documentation workshops**‚Äîeveryone had access to **technical references**

**Stakeholder management**: Collaborated with **PMs**, **data scientists**, **external teams**

**Empowerment**: **Team autonomy** while maintaining **alignment**

**Documentation**: **Comprehensive technical docs** for every project

Aligns with EA's need for **tech artists**, **content creators**, **data scientists**, **game engine programmers**."

### 8. "What are your salary expectations?"
**Answer**:
"Looking for **competitive package** reflecting **5+ years** building **cloud-native ML apps** at Amazon. 

Open to discussing **full comp**‚Äî**base**, **equity**, **benefits**. 

What range does EA typically offer?"

### 9. "What's your availability?"
**Answer**:
"**Available immediately**. Flexible with **hybrid** (**3 days/week in office**). Based in **Vancouver, BC**."

### 10. "Do you have any questions for me?"
**See Questions to Ask section below**

---

### Your AWS Expertise (Match to JD)
- **Lambda**: Serverless API development, event-driven architectures
- **SageMaker**: Model deployment (Endpoints, Batch Transform)

- **API Gateway**: RESTful API development and management
- **CloudWatch & X-Ray**: Monitoring, logging, distributed tracing

- Experience with OpenAI, Anthropic, Gemini, Ollama
- Vector databases, RAG, LLMs, model deployment

- **Backend**: Python (Flask, FastAPI), Node.js

- **APIs**: RESTful API design and implementation

### Your Documentation & Collaboration (Match to JD)

- "Robust documentation & operational readiness" recognition

- Cross-functional collaboration with multiple teams

### Your AI Development Tools (Match to JD)

- **MCP**: Model Context Protocol familiarity

| 4+ years cloud development | ‚úÖ 5+ years at Amazon building AWS cloud-native apps |
| Python + ML proficiency | ‚úÖ Built AI agents, RAG systems, NLP chatbots, ML pipelines |
| AWS services (Lambda, SageMaker, DynamoDB, API Gateway) | ‚úÖ Extensive: Led teams using Lambda, SageMaker, DynamoDB, API Gateway, Step Functions, CDK, CloudWatch |

## üìã Common HR Screen Questions & Answers

### 1. "Tell me about yourself"
**Answer (60-90 seconds)**:
- **Aviral Garg**. 5+ years at Amazon building **cloud-native ML apps**
  - Specialize in **full-stack AI solutions**
  - Using **AWS**: Lambda, SageMaker, DynamoDB, API Gateway

- At Amazon:
  - Led 8 engineers building **serverless pipelines**
    - Processing 40TB/day
    - Serving 40M+ customers monthly
  - Built **AI agents** for internal docs
    - Improved resolution time 82%
    - Saved 240+ dev-hours/month
    - Reached 100% documentation completion

- Recent focus: **AI development**
  - Voice assistants, real-time transcription, full-stack AI apps

- Excited about EA:
  - Combines **AI/ML**, **cloud**, creating experiences for millions of fans

### 2. "Why are you interested in Electronic Arts?"
**Answer**:
Three reasons:

- **Impact at scale**
  - EA games reach hundreds of millions globally
  - Grew up hearing "EA Sports, it's in the game"
  - Building ML cloud apps that enhance these experiences

- **Technical alignment**
  - Perfect match: Python, AWS (Lambda, SageMaker, DynamoDB), AI tools, full-stack, IaC
  - Built exactly these systems at Amazon

- **Collaboration**
  - Work with tech artists, data scientists, content creators, game devs
  - Deploy ML models, build automation pipelines
  - Aligns with my cross-functional experience

### 3. "Why are you leaving Amazon?" / "What have you been doing since March?"
**Answer**:
- **Laid off** March 2025
  - Organizational restructuring
  - Manager, manager's manager‚Äîall laid off
  - Beauty Tech team being merged

- After 5+ years, took opportunity to:
  - **Step back**, work on myself
  - Spend time with family
  - Good break

- Used time **productively**:
  - Deepened **ML/AI expertise**
    - Enrolled in ML program: EDA, Feature Engineering, Neural Networks, NLP, Agentic Frameworks
  - Built **full-stack AI apps**:
    - Voice assistants
    - Real-time transcription
    - Health misinformation prevention
    - Using AWS, Python, AI tools

- Now **energized** and ready
  - Want to build ML cloud apps for millions of fans

### 4. "What's your biggest accomplishment?"
**Answer**:
- At Amazon: built **AI agents** powered by internal docs
  - Answered CI/CD questions instantly
  - Improved resolution time 82%
  - Saved 240+ dev-hours/month

- **End-to-end ownership**:
  - Identified problem
  - Architected solution (Lambda, SageMaker)
  - Built RAG pipeline
  - Drove adoption org-wide

- Demonstrated: combining **ML/AI** with **cloud infrastructure**
  - Solve real business problems
  - Exactly what EA needs

### 5. "What's your experience with AWS services mentioned in the JD?"
**Answer**:
**Extensive hands-on**:

- **Lambda & API Gateway**: serverless APIs, data pipelines
- **SageMaker**: deployed ML models (Endpoints, Batch Transform)
- **DynamoDB**: session persistence, high-throughput storage
- **CloudWatch & X-Ray**: 4-stage CI/CD pipelines, granular monitoring
- **AWS CDK/CloudFormation**: Infrastructure-as-code, deployment pipelines
- **Cognito**: authentication systems
- **SAM & SSM**: serverless deployment, parameter management
- **Step Functions**: orchestrated workflows (40TB/day)

### 6. "What's your experience with AI tools like MCP, n8n, coding agents?"
**Answer**:
**Power user** of modern AI dev tools:

- **Coding agents**:
  - Daily: Cursor, Windsurf for AI-assisted development

- **MCP** (Model Context Protocol):
  - Familiar with architecture, use cases

- **n8n**:
  - Open-source workflow automation
  - Low-code automation pipelines
  - Connect APIs, databases, AI services ‚Üí intelligent workflows
  - Like Zapier but self-hosted, highly customizable

- **Generative AI**: OpenAI, Anthropic, Gemini, Ollama

- **Real-world**: Built 'Bob'‚ÄîAI voice assistant
  - 8 operational modes
  - Reduced costs 40x via prompt engineering

- Central to workflow, excited to accelerate EA's development cycles

### 7. "How do you handle working with cross-functional teams?"
**Answer**:
"At Amazon, led teams of **8 engineers**, **designers**, **data scientists**. 

**Key practices**:

**Clear communication**: Led **org-wide documentation workshops**‚Äîeveryone had access to **technical references**

**Stakeholder management**: Collaborated with **PMs**, **data scientists**, **external teams**

**Empowerment**: **Team autonomy** while maintaining **alignment**

**Documentation**: **Comprehensive technical docs** for every project

Aligns with EA's need for **tech artists**, **content creators**, **data scientists**, **game engine programmers**."

### 8. "What are your salary expectations?"
**Answer**:
"Looking for **competitive package** reflecting **5+ years** building **cloud-native ML apps** at Amazon. 

Open to discussing **full comp**‚Äî**base**, **equity**, **benefits**. 

What range does EA typically offer?"

### 9. "What's your availability?"
**Answer**:
"**Available immediately**. Flexible with **hybrid** (**3 days/week in office**). Based in **Vancouver, BC**."

### 10. "Do you have any questions for me?"
**See Questions to Ask section below**

### Your AWS Expertise (Match to JD)

- **SageMaker**: Model deployment (Endpoints, Batch Transform)

- **CloudWatch & X-Ray**: Monitoring, logging, distributed tracing

- **Cognito**: Authentication and authorization
- **SAM & SSM**: Serverless Application Model, Systems Manager
- **Step Functions**: Workflow orchestration

- Deployed NLP chatbots with full CI/CD
- Integrated OpenAI Whisper for local ML-based speech recognition
- Health misinformation prevention system with multi-agent simulation
- Experience with OpenAI, Anthropic, Gemini, Ollama
- Vector databases, RAG, LLMs, model deployment

### Your Full-Stack Expertise (Match to JD)

- **Backend**: Python (Flask, FastAPI), Node.js
- **Databases**: DynamoDB, PostgreSQL, SQLite
- **APIs**: RESTful API design and implementation

- **MCP**: Model Context Protocol familiarity

## üö® Red Flags to Avoid

‚ùå **Don't say**:
- Negative things about Amazon or previous employers
- "I don't have experience with X" (reframe as "I haven't used X specifically, but I've used similar tools like Y")
- Appear desperate or over-eager
- Discuss compensation too early (let them bring it up)

‚úÖ **Do say**:
- Specific examples with metrics (82% improvement, 240 dev-hours saved, 40TB/day)
- "That's a great question" (buy yourself thinking time)
- Ask clarifying questions if needed
- Express genuine excitement about EA's mission
